## Page 2

Publishers Note

This volume of Sarvarth Chintamani has been. sadly
over delayed due to the sudden demise of its renowned author
Sh. J.N. Bhasin. In his absence the Publishers had to over come
many difficulties, which, if he had been with us could have been
sorted out without any effort two years ago, The manual proofs
of over ‘hundred, pages had to be discarded as they distorted
the image, the learned author wanted to present. A scarch of
the original text in sanskrit had to be made; with help of
Shri 5.5. Sareen, but for whom the present form and shape could
have not been possible.He has not only edited the original
manuscript but revised and set them in order so that a presentable
shape to such a rare and ancient text could be provided with
English rendering, a long felt need of our readers.

The publisher experesses his heart felt gratitude to
Shri 9.9. Sareen, Shri Girish Chand Sharma & Shri Vivek Seth to
make the book what it is now before you.

## Page 4

INTRODUCTORY NOTE

(1) “Sarvarth Chintamani” is one of the top astrological works.
From the point of view of practical utility it offers very valuable
comments on the subjects relating to each of the 12 houses of a
birth chart. It has the unique distinction of following a procedure
where by the main subject or objects pertaining to a house are first
of all stated in the very beginning of the chapter relating to that
70५56 and then each of those subjects is dealt with in a suitable
astrological way on the basis of the house concerned, its lord and
its significator and the results—good and bad—declared.

(2) For example in the first shloka of chapter 3 dealing with the
affairs of the 2nd house of the horoscope the author—Shri
Venktesh Sharma has given family, dependents, mouth, speech,
right eye. accumulated wealth, education, eating, servents & friend
as the affairs covered by the 2nd house. He then deals with cach of
these affairs in detail. For example: He states that if a natural
benefic Planct occupies the 2nd house, and the lord of the 2nd is
also a natural benefic Planet and the significator—the Sun—is
under good influence the man has broad eyes with good sight.
Similar treatment is accorded to other affairs.

(3) On certain important points which required special men-
tion we have inserted our notes bringing out the value of that
specific point, with apt illustrations from actual life, It is hoped
these notes and illustrations will go a long way in bringing out the
true import of the shlokas.

(4) The aspects of Rahu and Ketu are conspicuous in this book
by their absence. But we have added suitable notes to fill in the
omission in this respect.

(5) It is our conviction that a birth chart having correct lon-
gitudes according to correct ayanamsa would give correct balance
of dasa. Divination carried out on the basis of such a dasa with due
regard to the aspects of the nodes and to the fu.ictioning of the
planets as dispositors. would give correct results when applied to
the house involved. the lord of that house & its significator.

(6) In regard to the use of correct ayanamsa we would recom-
mend on the basis of our experience that the value of the Shri
14111115 ayanamsa as applicable to a particular date should be

---

## Page 5

reduced by 1 degree and 7 minutes and the longitude of Moon then
arrived at should be used to ascertain the balance of dasa. In the
alternative the longitude of Moon according to Shri Lahiri should
be increased by | degree & 7 minutes & the balance of dasa
arrived.

J.N. Bhasin

Flat 1, Double Storey Market

New Rajendra Nagar

New Delhi

Author of Astro Sutras, Medical Astrology. Events & Nativities/
Art of Prediction.

SARVARTH CHINTAMANI
CHAPTER-1

श्रीमच्छेषगिरेस्तटाधिनिलयं श्रीवेंकटेश TE

नत्वा वेंकटनायकं तचनुदिन॑ जातोहमार्यात्सुधी : ।।

ज्योति : शास्त्र महान्धिपारगमने वक्ष्यामि पोतात्मकं

ज्योति : शास्त्र विवेक पाक विदुषां सर्वार्थचितामणिम ।। १ ।।

Shri Venket Sharma, the author, offers the followirlg opening
prayer (mangalacharanam):
“After bowing repeatedly to Lord Venketeshwar, who has his
abode on the side of the mountain called “Sheshadri™ and to the
most respectable Guru of mine whose grace has made me Pandit
Vyankat sharma. 1 offer the book “Sarvarth Chintamani” as a ship
to cross the Great ocean of Astrology by the people learned in the
art of astrological divination. (1)

नीलांबुजरुचिं देव सकृद्यांति मनोरथम्‌ ।।
देवा : प्रणम्य यं सर्वे तं नमामि गजाननम्‌ ।। २ ।।

1 bow to Shri Ganesh. who has the lustre like a blue Lotus and
by worshipping whom all the gods easily get their desired
object. (2)

वाग्विभूतिप्रदा देवी या श्वेतांबुरुइस्थिता ।।
गोक्षीरधवलाकारा स्वयं तिष्ठतु वाचि मरे ।। ३ ।।

May the Godess Sarasvati, who bestows on men the wealth of
speech. who has her abode in the white Lotus and whose comple-
\10011 is white like the Cow's milk, make my speech as her
abode. (3)

मेषादिराशयः सर्वे दिनेशप्रमुखा प्रहा: ।।
ये च लोकोपकर्तारः पातु मामिह ते सदा ।। ४ ।।

May the signs Aries etc. the Planets Sun etc and others engaged
in the welfare of mankind. always give me their protection. (4)

यज्जातके निगदितं भुवि मानवानां तत्प्राशिनिकेपि सकलं कथय॑ति तज्जाः ।।
प्रश्नोपि उन्मसदुशो भवति प्रभेदः प्रश्नस्य चात्र जननस्य न कश्चिदस्ति ।। ५ ।।

## Page 7

Nhatever principles have been enunciated in the Natal Astrology,
ire equally applicable to the "Horary™ Astrology. There is no dif-
erence between the two (Horary relates to chart of the heaven pre-
vared for the moment of query). (5)

भोमाच्छविच्चन्द्रविज्ञशुक्रंयक्रोज्यमदार्कसुतामरेज्या : ।।
मेषादिभ्रानामधिपा : क्रमेण तदैशकानामपि ते भवेयु : ।। ६ ।।

lhe lords of the 12 signs Aries to Pisces are Mars, Venus, Mercury,
Moon, Sun, Mercury. Venus, Mars, Jupiter, Saturn, Saturn and
lupiter respectively. The lord of a navamsa is the same as that of
he sign as stated above. (6)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

The idea underlying the lordship of the plantets over the signs is
‘0 state the fact that the various signs always act like the planets
having lordship over them. For details regarding Navamsha. (See
Shloka 11.)

मेषादिमूर्धा वदनं गलाधोह्त्कुक्षिवासोभृतबस्तिगुहम्‌ | |
ततोरुजानुदयजंघमंघ्री पापान्वितं यत्तदुपेति नाशम्‌ ।। ७ ।।

Aries represents head, Taurus face, Gemini breast, Cancer
heart, Leo belly, Virgo waist, Libra private parts, Scorpio rectum,
Sagittarius hips, Capricorn knees. Aquarius legs and Pisces feel.
The sign that is afflicted by the association etc of malefic Planets
denotes trouble in the limb it represents. (7)

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

The shloka is useful in the diagnosis of diseases of the limbs of
the body. The particular limb represented by the sign. of course
suffers as a result of affliction of the association or aspect on it of
malefic planets. But the results would be more palpable
if the lord of the sign also is afflicted. 11. in addition. the house rep-
resenting the limb is afficted. the disease or injury would be more
severe. 11 all the four factors representing a limb namely the sign.
its lord, the house comesponding in number to the sign and the lord of
that house are afflicted the trouble would be the severe most. The
nature of trouble in the limb and its severity also depend on the
severity of the affliction ie. on the number and strength of the
afflicting planets and their nature. For example. if the 5th sign and
its lord, the 5th house and its lord are influenced by Rahu and the

J

---

## Page 8

lord of the sign occupied by Rahu it would be a case of heart
attack. If by Saturn and by the lord of the sign occupied by Saturn
it would be a case of dyspepsia, indigestion etc. If by Mars and
Ketu or by the lords of the signs occupied by Mars and Ketu. it
would be a case for operation of or injury to the belly. In regard to
intensity it may be added that if for example. the 12th house. lord
of the 12th house sign number 12 and its lord Jupiter are all aflic-
ted by both Mars & Ketu or by Mars as lord of the sign occupied by
Ketu or by both, the feet may have to be amputated.

व्यत्यस्तमत्स्यदयमश्वजंघश्चापी मनुष्य : सगदं सवीणम्‌ | |
नृयुग्ममादाय करेग्निसस्ये नोस्थाबला मानधरो वणिक्‌ च ।। ८ ।।
घटी जलादानग्रहीतुकाम : शेषा : स्वनामानुगुणा भर्वति ।।

मेषस्तु मेषो वृषभ : स एव कर्की कुलीरस्त्वथ वृश्चिकोलि : ।। ९ ।।

The sign Pisces is symbolised by two fish with the tail of one on
the mouth of the other, Sagittarius by a man with the lower portion
as of a horse and with bow in the hand. Gemini by a pair of man
and woman, holding mace and the musical instrument-veena.
Virgo by a girl in a boat. holding a fire pot in one hand and grains
in the other. Libra by a man with balance in the hand, Aquarius by
a man carrying on his shoulder a water pot. The traits of the rest of
the signs are as denoted by their names i.e. Aries by lamb, Taurus
by an ox. Cancer by crab. the sca creature of that name, Scorpio by
Scorpion. (8-9)

राशि त्रिघाकृत्य दुकाणमाहुस्तदीशपुत्रेश शुभाधिनाथा : ।।
युजीन्दुसूय्यीं भवने रवीन्दु नाथो त्वयुग्मे भवनस्य चाद्रे ।। १० ।।

A decante (Drikaan) consists of one third part of a sign. The first
decante i.e. from degrees | to 10 has the same planet as its lord as
the lord of the sign whose Ist decante it is. The 2nd decante from
degrees 11 to 20 is owned by the planet who is lord of the sign Sth to
the sign under consideration. The 3rd decante from 21 to 30
degrees is owned by the planet lord of the sign 9th to that under
consideration. In even signs the lord of the first hora i.e. the first 15
degrees is Moon & of the next is the Sun, while in the case of odd
signs the hora of the first half of the sign belongs to the Sun & the
second half to Moon. (10)

चरंशका नामधिपास्तदशाद्राशौ स्थिरे तन्नवमेश्वराद्या : ।।
दिदेहमेतत्सुतराशिनाधाद्रदैति शास्त्रार्थविदो महांत : ।। ११ ।।

The first Navamsha sign in the cardinal signs 1, 4. 7. & 10 is the
lord of the sign itself i.e. Mars, Moon, Venus & Saturn respectively.

5

---

## Page 9

The first Navamsha sign in the fixed signs 2, 5, 8 and 11 are the
signs 9th from the sign i.e. 10, 1, 4 and 7 respectively. The first
Navamsa sign in signs 3. 6.9 & 12 are the signs fifth from the sign
Le. 7, 10. 1 & 4 respectively. (The rest follow in the order as stated in
shloka-6.) (11)

TRANSLATORS NOTE

Since the order of the Navamsha signs is the same as in the
natural order Aries Taurus etc to Pisces there is a very simple way
to find out the Navamsha sign. Suppose we desire to find out the
Ist Navamsha sign in the sign Gemini. Multiply the number of
signs past i.e. 2 by 9. The result gives the signs past i.c. 18 or Virgo
(12 plus 6) hence the first sign in Gemini would be the sign next to
Virgo ie. Libra.

Example 2 Find out the sign representing the 4th Navamsha of
Sagittarius. Here 8X9 = 72 plus 4 = 76 divided by 12 leaves 4 i.e.
the answer & lord of 4 ie. Moon is the lord of the 4th
Navamsha of Sagittarius.

We give below tables showing the signs falling in the various
vargas or divisions of a sign and the lord of the signs so
falling

तत्क्ेत्रपा द्वादशभागनाथा लग्रस्य वर्गाधिपतिस्तदीशात्‌ | |
त्रिशांशपा भोमशनीज्यसौम्यशुक्रा भवैत्योजगृहे समे तु ।। १२ ।।

विलोमत : पंचशराष्टसप्तबाणा : क्रमादचुरनेकशास्त्रे : ।।
सप्तांशपास्त्वोजगृहे तदीशायुग्मे गृहे सप्तमराशिपात्तु ।। १३ ।।

The Ist 1/12th part of a sign belongs to the sign itself & the other
parts come in the order of the signs. As regards the 30th part. in the
odd signs the lords of the first 5 degrees is Mars, of the 6th to 12th
degrees Saturn, of the 13th to 20th degrees Jupiter. of the 21st to
25th degrees Mercury. of the 26th to 30th Venus. In the even signs
the order is reverse i.e. the first 5 degrees belong to Venus. 6th to
10th to Mercury, 11th to 18th to Jupiter. 19th to 25th to Saturn &
26th to 30th to Mars.

In odd signs the lord of the first 1/7th division is the lord of the
sign itself & in even signs the lord of the 151 1/7th division is the
lord of the sign 7th to the sign involved. The order of the signs
remaining as the natural one. This table has already been given

दशांशपानामधिपास्तदीशादोजे समे तन्नवमेश्वराद्या : ।।

ओजे कलानामधिपास्तदीशाश्चतुर्मुखो विष्णुहरौ दिनेश : ।। १४ ।।
युग्मे क्रमाव्यत्ययमेव राशौ षष्टथंशपानामधिपास्त्वयुग्मे ।। १५ ।।

In the odd signs the first 1/10th division belongs to the lord of
the sign itself and in even signs the Ist 1/10th division belongs to
the lord of the sign counted 9th from it. The order of signs is
natural one. The lords of these divisions are the 10 dik pals (lords
of directions). In the 1/16th division the lords of the divisions are
the lords of the signs Aries to Pisces & then Aries to Cancer. In the
sign Taurus the signs would be 5 to 12 & then | to 8 & so on (See the
table). (14, 15)

अथ प्रसंगादिं शांशसिद्धांशमांशचत्वारिं शांशपंचवेदांशा : । तत्रादौ विंशांश : ।

अथ विशति भागानामधिपा ब्रह्मणोदिता : ।। क्रियाच्चरे स्थिरे चापान्मृगेद्रादिदस्व-
भावके ।। १ ।। काली गौरी जया लक्ष्मीविजया विमला सती ।। तारा ज्वालामुखी

सुमुखी चेति विषमे परिचितयेत्‌ ।। ३ ।। समराशो दया मेधा छिन्नशीर्षा
पिशाचिनी ।। धूमावती च मातेगी बला भद्रारुगानला ।। ४ ।। पिंगला छुछुका घोरा

## Page 17

नक्षत्रेशस्तु भांशेशा : भांशसंख्या : स्वभात्‌ क्रमात्‌ ।। ११ ।। उदाहरणम- यथा
लग्नं ३। ८। ४५ मकरादरणनया सिंह आगत एवं सर्वत्र जेयम्‌ | | अथ खवेदाशंगणना ।।
| चत्वारिशद्विभागानामधिपा विषमे क्रियात्‌ ।। विष्णुचन्द्रौ मरीचिश्च त्वष्टा धाता
शिक रवि : ।। १२ ।। यमो यक्षेशगंघवों कालो वरूण एव च ।। समभे तुलतो
ज्ञेया : स्वस्वाधिपसमन्विता : ।। १३ ।। उदाहरणम्‌- यथालग्न ३-८-४५
तुलादिगणनीया : कन्या आगता : एवं सर्वत्र ज्ञेयम्‌ ।। अथाक्षवेदांशम्‌ ।।
तथाक्ववेदमागानामधिपाश्चरमे क्रियात्‌ ।। स्थिरेसिहाददिस्वभावे चापाब्द्रद्येशकेशवा : ।।
ईशाच्युतसुरेज्येष्टविष्णुकेशाश्चरादिषु ।। १४ ।।

उदाहरणम्‌ | यथा लग्नम्‌ ३। ८। ४५। मेषाब्दरणनया वृष आगत : एवं सर्वत्र ज्ञेयम्‌ ।। »

In the 1/24th division the signs from Aries & other odd signs
start with Leo. In the case of even signs these start with Cancer as
shown in the table.

As regards the 1/27th division the Ist 27th division of the sign
Aries belongs to Aries. 2nd 27th division to the next sign & so on,
till the 27th which will in this order be governed by Gemini. Hence
the 1st 27th division of Taurus will be governed by Cancer & so on.
In the 1/40th diyision, the first division in all odd signs belongs to
the sign Aries; while in all even signs, it belongs to Libra, as shown
in the table. In the 1/45 division, the 1st division of every movable
sign belongs to Aries; the 1st of every fixed sign, to Leo and the first
of every common sign, to Sagittarius. The order of the signs owned
remains the natural one. (6-14)

In the case of the 1/60th division, the Ist and the 2nd division
belongs to the sign itself, the 3rd and the 4th division belongs to the
next sign(?), the Sth & 6th division belongs to the next sign i.e. to
Gemini and so on as shown in the table. If a particular division is
associated with a benefic Planet, the results given by the Planets
are good. (15-20)

## Page 28

्ररषष्टधशगा : सर्वे नाशय॑ति खचारिण : ।। यदि पूर्णबलै्युक्ता : स्वोच्वमूल-
त्रिकोणगा : ।। २१।। स्व्केन््रोत्तमांशस्था  मित्रक्षेत्रत्रकिणगा : ।। सप्त-
वर्गोदभाःवा : स्वांशा : स्वाधिमित्रांशकान्विता : ।। २२ ।।

Planet with full strength such as by being in exaltation, in posi-
tive sign, but located in a malefic 1/60th division gets harmed (21)
A planet in its own sign, in kendra, in friendly sign, in positive sign,
located 11 its own sign in the 7 vargas, in a bosom friends sign is
called "uttam” (best). (22)

वगस्तु ये दश प्रोक्ता : पूर्वाचायर्महार्षिभि : ।। भवंति वर्गसंयोगे पारिजातादि
संज्ञका : ।। २३ ।। दुः स्थारिनीचमूटस्था ग्रहा बलविवर्जिता : ।। मरणावस्थगाश्चेत्त
पारिजातादिनाशका : ।। २४ ।।

The ancient Acharyas and Maharshis have mentioned ten fold
division of the longitudes of planets etc. They have termed the
number of vargas or division obtained as “Parijat” etc. Planets
which are located in bad houses 1.6. 6th, 8th & 12th, in their inimi-
cal sign or in their debilitation sign or are eclipsed by the Sun or
are otherwise weak by being in *‘Maranavastha' i.e. in the end of a
sign, destroy the good results arising out of the good vargas or
divisions got by them through their longitude. (23, 24)

उत्तमं तु त्रिवर्गैक्यं चतुर्वर्ग तु गोपुरम्‌। । वर्गपंचकसंयोगे सिंहासनमिहोच्यते।।२५।।
वर्गद्रयं पारिजातं षण्णां पोरावतांशकम्‌।। सप्तमं देवलोकं स्यादेष्टमं चामरं
भवेत्‌।।२६।। एेरावतं तु नवमं फलं तेषां पृथक्पृथक।। दशवर्गस्य संयोगे
विदुर्वेशेषिकांशकान्‌। ।२७।।

If in the longitude of the planet etc there are two beneficial
divisions, it is called “Paarijaat™. If 3, it is called “Uttam”, if 4
“Gopur”, if 5 “Simhaasan”, if 6 "Paaraavat” if 7“Devlok”, if 8
“Amar, if 9 “Airaavat”, & if 10 it is called “Vaisheshik™. The
results of these are different (see next shloka). (25-27)

ठेरावते सार्वभौम : सर्वैश्वर्यसमन्वित : ।। देवलोके महादानकर्ता राजा
क्षितीश्वर : ।।२८।। पारावते माण्डलिक : सर्वशास्प्रविशारद : ।। सिंहासने
भवेदमूमियति : सर्वै : स्तुतो महान्‌।।२९।। गोपुरे घनवान्नित्य॑ सर्वविद्या-
विशारद : ।। उत्तमे सकला संपत्‌ पारिजाते धनान्वित : ।।३०।। स्वांशे यशस्वी
मतिमान्‌ सर्वसौख्य समन्वित : ।।३१।।

In the case of “Airaavat” division one becomes emperor, in

"Devlok™ one is highly charitable, in “Paaraavat” one is king
‘knowing all sciences & arts, if in “Simhaasan”. One is the object of

## Page 29

praise every where, in “Gopur” one is wealthy & a man of allround
knowledge, if in “Uttam” one has all kinds of wealth & if in “Pari-
jat” one is fairly rich. If the planet has thc division denoting his
own sign the native is famous, intelligent, and leads a confortable
life. (28-31)

लग्न क्रमात्सा्दघटीदरयं स्यान्मेषाहिंनेशस्थितकोणभानाम। | राशीश्वरात्प्राणपदै क्रमेण
घटीचतुर्थाशमुशंति तज्ज़ा : ।।३२।। चापाद्विपर्येति रविस्तु साई घटीद्वयं रात्रिकरौगि
तस्मात्‌।। क्रमेण साईदयनाडिकाल : कुजे वृषाव्यत्ययनाडिमात्रम्‌। 1331 +
चापाद्बुधो व्यत्ययनादिमात्रं मीनादध .: पंचघटीन्द्रपूज्य : ।। क्रमेण युग्मादपृ-
गुनन्दनस्तु घटीप्रमाणो दिननायपुत्र : ।।३४।। व्यत्यासमार्गेण घटीप्रमाणो मेषादगु .
साईघटीयुगं स्यात्‌! । मीनाच्छिखी तन्मदगो विलोमाच्छास्त्रांतरे तत्फलमाुरः
SEL SN

The duration of each of the 12 signs from Aries is two & a hail
ghati. Thus cach sign comes twice in a day of 24 hours. This 15
} called hora lagna. “Pranpad is the sign arrived at by converting the
Ishta i.e. time elapsed from the last Sunrise to the moment of birth
as the Palas & dividing the palas by 15. The result would be signs
and degrees etc. These signs etc added to the longitude of the Sun if
located in a movable sign gives the location point of Pranpad. In
case the Sun 15 not located in a movable sign but in a fixed one the
movable sign 9th to the one arrived at by taking Sun in a movable
sign should be taken & in case the Sun occupies a commen sign
the sign Sth to it should be taken as containing the Pran Pada. For
cxample supposing Sun has the longitude 9° 28° 30. & the Ishte is 2
ghatis & 16 palas the 2 ghatis & 16 palas are 136 palas, which
divided by 15 gives 9 ayns & 2 degrees, which added to 9 26 30) (A
movable sign) gives 19-0-30 = 7-0-30 as Pran Pada point (3.
The Sun comes back two & a half Ghatis from Sagittarius So
also is the case with Moon. Mars comes only one ghati in opposite
direction. Mercury comes only one ghati in opposite direction.
Jupiter 15 5 ghatis in opposite direction of Pisces. Venus cores
after 2 ghatis from Pisces & Saturn after | ghatis. Rahuis | ghatiin
opposite direction from Arics. Ketu comes 7th to Rahu: The res: lis
of these positions are laid down in other works. (32-35)

बालायावस्था : क्रमशो ग्रहाणामोजे समे तद्विपरीतमाहु : ।

बाल : कुमारो युवा च वृद्दो मृतो लवानामृतुमि : क्रमेण।।२६।।

बालाय वस्थानुगुणं व्रजंति तत्पाककाले दिननायमुख्या : ।। २७1 ;

The above shlokas 33 to 35 are not quite clear. Nor 15 it known as
to where there explanation appears.

## Page 30

Planets located in odd signs are (symbolically) given the names,
“child” "boy" “youth” "old" & “dead” when occupying the degrees
1 (0 6, 7 to 12. 13 to 18, 19 to 24 & 25 to 30 respectively in the
occupied sign. If they are located in even signs the names for the 5
states involved are given in the reverse oider i.e. “Death”, “Old”,
“Youth”, “Boy” & "Child" respectively. Planets in their ruling
periods give their results with a strength in keeping with the age
specified (35. 37).

मेषाजवस्तं प्रथमं क्रियश्च वृषोक्षगोतावुरिशुक्रभं च ।।२८।।
बोधं नृयुग्म॑ जितुमं तृतीयं च्रं कुलीरं तु चतुर्धराशिम ¦
सिंहस्य कंठीरवलेपसंज्ञा पाथोनषष्टी त्ववला च तन्वी ।।३९।।
जूके वणिक्सप्तमतोलिसंज्ञ : कौप्योष्टम॑ कोजमलेस्तु संज्ञा : |
जवं धनुस्तोक्षिकचापसंजञं त्वाकेकरं स्याद शमं च चक्रम्‌ 11501
द्द्रोगकुम्भो घटराशिसंजे मीनो झषश्चांतिमरिष्फसंज्ञ : ।।४१।।

The synonyms of the various sign in the Sanskrit language are:
Aries is called Meshaj, Vasta Pratham, kriy; Taurus is called
Vrishabha, Uksha, Go, Tavari, Shukra Bham (sign of Venus)
Gemini is called Mithun, Baudh, Nriyugma, Jitum, Triteeya, Can-
cer 15 called Karka, Chaandram, kuleer, chaturth, Leo is called
Simha, Kanthirav, Leya, Virgo is called Kanya Pathon, Shashti, &
Abala, Libra is called Jook, Vanik, Saptam, Tula, & Tauli, Scorpio
is calied Kaurpya, Ashtam, Vrishchik kauj, & Ali, Sagittarius is
called Jaiva, Dhanu, Taukshik, chaap, Capricorn is called
Aakekar Dasham, Caakra, & Makar, Aquarius is calicd Hndrog,
Kumbha, Ghat, Pisces is called Rishph. Mcena, Jhash, Antim, &
Meena (38 & 41).

SYNONYMNS FOR HOUSES

The first house is named as hora, tanu, (body) moorti, (comple-
xion) udaya, (rising) shir, (head). The second is called vaag
(speech), vitta (wealth), kutumba (family), eye. The 3rd is called
sahotha (brother), dushchikya. gala (throat). The 4th is called
shourya (bravery), karna (ears). sukha, water, bandhu (comforts,
nater & friend & relatives) rasatal (nadir) hibuk (chest) veshma
(residence), patal (nadir) hrid (heart), vahan (conveyance) matri
(mother). The Sth is called budhi (intellect), prabhav (influence),
aatmaj (son), mantra (advisory capacity), vivek (discrimination),
udar (belly). The 6th is called disease, kshat (injury), ari (enemies),
vysanam (addiction), chor (theft), vighana (obstacles). The 7th is
called chittoth, kaam, madan (sexual urge), wife, bhrtri (husband),
dadih, (curd) soup. The 8th is called ksheer (milk) gudam (gur)
montra kricha (urinary trouble), goohya (hidden) randhra (bad)
marana anta (death) Aayou (age). The 9th is termed as dharma
(duty), daya (compassion) paitrik (father) bhagya (luck), guru
(preceptor) tapas (penance) laabh (gains) shubhaarjitaani(earned
merit). The 10th is termed as aagya (orders) maan (honour)
dashma (tenth) karma (actions) aspad (position) kham (sky). The
[1th is termed as ayam & laabh (gains). The 12th is termed as
vyaya (expenditure) antya (last sign) rishpha (bad) vinash (des-
truction) (42-46)

दुःस्थाश्च नाशप्रभवा भवंति षष्ठाष्टरिष्फानुगतास्तथैव |

उद्यति पृष्ठेन वृषाजचापकुलीरनक्रा बलिन : सयुग्मा : ।।४७।।
ते रात्रिकालेन्हि बलास्तु शेषा : शीर्षोदया मीनमुदेत्युभाभ्याम्‌ ।।४८।।

Planets located in the 6th. 8th or 12th house lose their influence.
So also is the case with the houses whose lords occupy these three
houses. The signs Aries, Taurus, Gemini, Cancer, Sagittarius and
Capricorn are called “Prishtodaya™ signs i.e. Rising with their
hind part and are strong in charts with night birth. Signs Leo,
Virgo, Libra, Scorpio, Aquarius & Pisces are strong in birth chart
for day birth. These are called. "Sheershodaya™ signs i.e. those
which rise with their front part But the sign Pisces rises in both
ways ie. with fore as well as hind part. (47-48)

iE विश्वभागश्रुतिभवनयुतो म॑डलाच्छोधितोसो पात : षड़ाशियुक्त : परिधिरथ
भसंशोधितश्चपनामा ।

शैलाशभागयुक्तं घनुरथ च शिखी पंच ते त्वप्रकाशा : प्रादुभवि च तेषां फल मिह कथितं
आतकप्रश्नयो : स्यात्‌ ।।४९।। इति प्रकाशग्रहा : ।।

28

---

## Page 32

By adding 13 degrees 20 minutes to the longitude of the Sun in
the birth chart we get the longitude of the space point called
“dhoom™. By deducting from 12 signs the longitude of dhoom we
get the remainder as the longitude of the space point called "paat™
or vyatipat”. By deducting 6 signs from this longitude we get the
longitude of the space point called “paridhi” or “parivesh”. By
deducting parivesh from 12 signs we get remainder as “chaap” or
“dhanu” by adding 16 degrees and 40 minutes to Dhanu we get
Ketu. By adding 2 signs to Keiu we get again the longitude of the
Sun with which we started. (49)

व्योमास्तपातालविलग्नभानां वदेति नामानि सुनीन्द्रजाला : ।
तत्क॑टकं केन्द्रचतुष्टयं च व्गोतमास्तत्स्वनवांशकास्तु ।।५०।।

The wise term the Ist, 4th, 7th & "10th houses as kendras,
chatushtayas, etc. If a Planet occupies the Navamsha of the same
sign in which it is located it is called “Vargottam™ (a vargottam
planet gives good results). (50)

जलचरपशुनरकीटा ब॑धौ माने तनौ मदे चापि ।
क्रमशो भवेति वीर्या विगतबलास्तत्सप्तमे वापि ।।५१।।

The watery signs (second half of Capricorn. Aquarius and Pis-
ces) are strong when located in the 4th house. The animal signs
(Aries, Taurus and Leo), the first half of Capricorn and 2nd half of
Sagittarius) are strong when located in the 10th house. The human
signs (Gemini, Virgo & Libra and Ist half of Sagittarius) are strong
in the Ist house and the insect signs (Cancer and Scorpio) are
strong when located in the 7th house. The signs, located in the 7th
house from where they get strength, are without strength. In the
intermediary position their strength is proportional. (51)

मेषोक्चनक्रांगनकार्किंमीनतुलाघरा : स्युदिनपात्स्वतुंगा : |
उत्युच्वमागैर्नयनागदारमत्यामनासारनरे : क्रमेण ।।५२।।
सिंहोक्षव स्तांगनचापतोलिकुंभा भवंत्युच्वसमान भावा : ।
मलत्रिकोणानि भवंति तानि किचिद्विहीनानि बलानि सूर्यात्‌ ।।५३।।
Sun 15 in its highest exaltation in the 10th degree of Aries, Moon
in the 3rd degree of Taurus, Mars in the 28th degree of Capricorn.
Mercury in 15th degree of Virgo, Jupiter in Sth degree of Cancer.

Venus in the 27th degree of Pisces, Saturn in the 20th degree of
Libra.

The mooltrikon or positive sign for the Sun is Leo; for Moon.
Taurus; for Mars, Aries; for Mercury, Virgo; for Jupiter. Sagit-

29

---

## Page 33

tarius: for Venus. Libra and for Saturn Aquarius. Planets in their
positive signs are very strong, only a little less than when in exalta-
tion. (52.53)

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

A question may be raised as to why a particular Planet gets
exalted in a particular sign & degree. So far as we are aware no
author has answered this question. We, however. think that this
can be explained on the basis of spirituality to which astrology
owes allegience being its main limb. The 10th degree of Aries falls
in the asterism Ashvini whose lord is Ketu. Ketu has been declared
by astrology as the "Moksha" karka i.e. the significator lor salva-
tion. The Sun is very well krown as the “Atma” in the Vedas.

(सूर्य : आत्मा जगतस्तस्थुषश्च)

Thus Sun in the 10th degree of Aries means Atma in Moksha.
obviously the highest state that the Atma can aspire to. Thus the
exaltation of Sun in the 10th degree of Aries 15 perfectly in con-
sonance with the spiritual principles. Now, why is Sun exalted in
Aries & not in Leo or Sagittarius, for if availability of Ketu is the
criterion, this asterism is equally available in Leo & Sagittarius.
The answer to this part of the question is that Leo and Sagittarius
belong to the “Satvik™ Sun and Jupiter. The signs of these planets
can hardly constitute a testing ground for the exalted Sun. Itis only
the sign of the sinful Mars which can offer a suitable testing
ground for the purpose, for Atma in Mcksha is untouched by
sin.

(2) Moon is exalted in the 3rd degree of Taurus. This degree falls
in the asterism "Kritika” belonging to the Sun. The Moon is mind.

(चन्द्रमा मनसो जात :)

Mind immersed in the Atma represents the highest state of
Samadhi. Nothing higher can be desired for the mind. Hence the
exaltation in the asterism “Kritika”. Now, why Taurus is preferred
when the asterisms of Sun are available in the signs 5.6.9, & 10?
The answer is that none of these four signs offer an emotional &
luxurious testing gound as does the sign Taurus—the sign of the
luxurious and amorous Venus. Hence the choice. Mars is exalted
in the 28th degree of Capricorn in the: asterism “"Dhanishta™
belonging to Mars himself. We know from astrology that Marsis a
great martial planet. For a solidier to retain his mettle & bravery.
even when surrounded by enemies in the enemy's camp. is his
highest attainment. This is exactly what happens when Mars
occupies Capricorn—the sign of its bitter enemy. Saturn. Hence

30

---

## Page 34

the justification for exaltation in Capricorn. The asterism of Mars,
no doubt, is also available in the signs 2.3.6.7 & 11; but Mercury.
the boy & Venus, the neutral can hardly test the bravery of Mars
through their signs. As regards Aquarius, Mars in Capricorn is
more strong than in Aquarius. In Capricorn it is near the asterism
of Mars while it is near that of Rahu in Aquarius.

(3) Mercury gets exalted in the 15th degree of Virgo. This degree
falls in the asterism “Hasta” belonging to Moon. Now Mercury is a
highly intellectual planet. Its intellect is a great asset. But too much
of intellect can ruin man as we have seen in the developement of
the Atom Bomb. It is therefore highly desirable that intellect
should be compassionate also. If it can be so nothing more can
make intellect exalted. This is exactly what happens when Mer-
cury in its own sign still retains compassion by being in the
asterism of Moon. Here again the point is that the asterism of
Moon is available in the signs 2 & 10. Why has Virgo been given
preference over signs 2 & 10? The answer is that in none of these
signs Mercury retains its intellectual eminence. It is only by retain-
ing intellect with compassion that Mercury can be considered as
exalted. Hence the justification.

(4) Jupiter gets exalted in the 5th degree of Cancer, belonging to
the asterism “Pushya” whose lord is Saturn. Jupiter is the
significator of wealth. Hence it has plenty of riches. It is also the
most spiritual planet. Hence it is fed up with wealth. It believes in
the maxim that man does not live by bread alone. Hence its aim 15
spiritual Samadhi. which is a state of "Shoonya™ or absence of
matter. This state is afforded easily by Saturn. Hence Jupiter gets
exalted in the asterism Pushya. Here again emotions & desires are
hinderances to Samadhi. Jupiter's exaltation is tested in the
emotional sign of Cancer. No other sign affords Samadhi and
emotional ground. Hence Cancer is most appropriate.

(5) Venus gets exalted in 27th degree of Pisces which falls in the
asterism Revati belonging to Mercury. Venus, a most luxury loving
and sensuous planet, is normally averse to the precepts of the shas-
tras denoted by Jupiter. But when he gets the spiritual intellect of
Mercury he gets changed spiritually & then Pisces constituting a
testing ground for him no longer remains a problem for him. No
other sign containing the asterism of Mercury is religious enough
10 offer a testing ground to Venus.

(6) Saturn is exalted in the 20th degree of Libra. The degree falls
in the asterism “Swati” belonging 10 Rahu. Saturn, the yogi, is in
his best element in the friendly congenial asterism of Rahu which
31

-

---

## Page 35

also stands for void Thus Saturn is still poor in spirit & 15 not
tempted by being in the luxurious, rich & sensuous sign Libra.

दिवाबला मानुषराशय : स्यू रात्रौ बलाटधा : पशवश्च कीटा : |
संध्यादरये भ्रातुभवास्पदानां सषष्ठभानां तु चयेति संज्ञा ।।५४।।

Human signs (3.6.7 & 1st half of 9) are strong in birth charts of
day birth. Animal signs (1,2,5 1st half of Capricorn and 2nd half of
Sagittarius) are strong during the night births. Inscct signs (4 and
8) are strong in the morning and evening time. The 3rd, 6th, 10th
and the 11th houses are commonly called “Chaya” or “*Upchaya”
houses. (54)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

The term “Chaya” or “Upchaya” means houses that gather the
traits of the planets located in them are said to be gained by the
native. This is particularly true for planets in the 10th & 11111
houses. For example, one gets many animals if Saturn (which
denotes animals) is located in the 11th house. The author of
Bhavarth Ratnakar holds (see shloka 1 under Libra lagna) that
Jupiter for Libra nativities gives good wealth in his dasa even
though Jupiter owns two bad houses of the horoscope. The reason
is that the element of “financial gain” as upchaya house 15 com-
mon between these houses & Jupiter.

officials. Mars is connected with the military. Mercury is heir

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

How the Planets, Jupiter and Venus. perform the functions of
ministers is illustrated by the Horoscope of Late Sanjay Gandhi.
His Horoscope (birth 14th Dec 1946) is reproduced below. It

would be observed that Venus, the minister, is lord of the house of
Mantrana or ministership viz.. the Sth from lagna. Similarly
Jupiter, the other minister, is the lord of the Sth house from the
Chandra Lagna. Both are located in the foremost kendra (10th)
denoting karma. Hence the active interest that Shri Sanjay
Gandhi showed in the affairs of the day to day working of the
government as an advisor. Even though holding no- portfolio
bears out the qualities of Jupiter & Venus as advisors to
government. |

सत्त्वाश्रय : सर्वगुणाभिराम : पिगाक्षमूर् न्यकचाभिराम : ।

स्थूलद्विजस्तामसबुद्वियुक्तो वातात्मको वाक्कठिनस्तु निंद्य : |

बलेन निशिचत्य षदेदग्रहाणां तत्प्राशिनिके जन्मनि तद्गुणास्तु ।।७२।।
TRAITS OF PLANETS

The Sun has a square body. Its colour is dark red, the lustre of.
his eyes is yellow, has the body humour of bile., of average length
in the bodily stature, has prowess, is satvik in nature, has very little
hair (66) is intimately linked to causing movements, possesses a
speech which gives meaning in very few words, gives very little, his
intellect is divinely oriented,

Moon is of white body. of average size, well at speech, with
round body. has the power of right thinking, is somewhat (67)
weak in body, has pleasing speech. is satvik in temperament,
possesses all the three humours ie. bile, phlegm & wind.

Mars has eyes red with anger, has body whitish red in colour,
possesses 0112 i.e. has heated nature, has haughty temperament, ‘is
thin of body, is prone to sin, has prowess, is given to sexual
pleasures.

Mercury is of the colour of green grass, is highly learned, is
ambitious, truthful in speech. (68) He is jocular, possesses all the
three humours bile, phlegm & wind, gives status etc., with quick-
ness, & is impotent. (69)

Jupiter is of satvik temperament, is endowed with all the good
qualities of character, has yellow eyes, has no hair on the head.

Venus has beautiful eyes, is sexy in nature, gives comforts,
strength, & beautiful complexion. (70)

Venus has black coloured hair on his body is ambitious in
nature, is endowed with all the good qualities.

Saturn is cruel, with a thin long body, yellow eyes. & hard hair.
(71) He has big sized teeth, is tamasic in nature (full of inertia)
causes wind i.e. nervous troubles, is curt in speech, & is despicable.
The results of the planets should be declared after due considera-
tion of their strength whether it is the domain of natal astrology or
of the horary astrology. (72)

CASTES OF PLANETS

Jupiter and Venus are brahmins, the Sun and Mars are kshat-
riyas or of the warrior class. Moon & Mercury belong to the trad-
ing community, Saturn belongs to shuddra, Rahu and Ketu
represent the lower most strata of one's community. Mandi rep-
resents a foreign community other than the set of communities in
which one is born. (73. 74)

Sun is red coloured. Moon is white, Mercury green, Jupiter
yellow, Venus of variegated colour, Saturp is blue. The devata of

PLACES & CLOTHES OF PLANETS

Sun (being satvik) 15 intimately linked to the Dev Sthaan i.e. the
temple etc, Moon to watery resorts, Mars to fiery places, Mercury
(being kumar ie. boy) to play grounds, Jupiter (being the
significator of wealth) to treasury etc, Venus (being sexy) to the bed
room, Saturn to uneven places, Rahu to holes of serpents etc. (79)
If Saturn represents a cloth, it would be old; if Sun, it would be
gross; if Jupiter, it would be neither old nor new; if Venus, it would
be strong; if Moon, new; if Mercury, it would be wet, if Mars, it
would be partially burnt, if Rahu, it would be old & of various
colours like the cloth of a poor menicant; if Ketu, it would be with
many holes. (81)

NATURE OF LOST THINGS, TASTE, TIME ETC

In horary astrology. in natal astrology or when the question of
reconstructing a horoscope without the birth data is invol red the
data is ascertained from the nature of the planets who are the lords
of the decantes involved. Among the tastes, the Sun represents the
Pungent taste, Mars the bitter, Moon the saltish. Mercury the
mixed one, Jupiter the sweet, Venus sour & Saturn astringent. In
periods of time, the Sun represents a period of six months, Moon
only a second. Mars a day, (89) Mercury a period of two months.
Jupiter a month, Venus a fortnight & Saturn a year. Rahu rep-
resents a period of 8 months & Ketu only 3 months.

Rahu, Saturn, Moon and Mars are planets representing Dhatu
i.e. metals. Sun and Venus represent planets, Jupiter and Mercury

Ashvini, Bharni & Kritika are metals, plants & Animals respec-

Rohini, Mrigshar & Ardra are metals. plants & Animals & so
on. (90)

## Page 42

पश्यत्यसौ भानुसुतस्तृतीयं मानं च पूर्ण चतुरक्षमार |
जीवस्त्रिकोणं मदनं च सर्वे पश्यंति दृष्टथा TOWER ।।९२।।

ASPECTS

Saturn fully aspects i.e. influences the house, sign or planet’
placed 3rd and 10th from it. Mars similarly aspects the house etc.
placed 4th and 8th from it. Jupiter similarly throws its influence on
the house etc Sth and 9th from it. All the planets aspect the 7th
house etc from the place of their location. The planets aspect the
3rd & 10th place from their places with quarter aspect. the place etc
5th & 9th from them with half aspect & the house etc 4th & 8th
from them with three quarters aspect. The house numbers should
be counted by taking the aspecting planet as in first house. (92)

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

Most of the astrological texts do not prescribe any aspects for
Rahu and Ketu. They omit it at their own peril. Maharshi
Parashar—the father of Indian astrology—has very clearly laid
down that Rahu and Ketu have aspects mostly similar to Jupiter
i.e. on the house etc Sth, 7th & 9th from them.

In this connection please see the following shloka (number 26 in
chapter 51) of Brihat Parashar Hora Shastra Bombay edition of
Shaka 1837.

सुतमदन नवान्ते पूर्ण दृष्टि तपस्य युगल दशम गेहे चार्धं इष्टिं वदन्ति
सहज रिचु विपश्यन्पाद दृष्टि मुनीन्द्रा : निजभवनपुपेतो लोचनान्ध : प्रदिष्ट :

i.e. Rahu has full aspect on the house etc located Sth, 7th, 9th and
12th from it. It has half the aspect (influence) on the houses 2nd
and 10th from it. It aspects with a quarter strength the house etc 3rd
and 6th from it and is blind towards the house it occupies.

Since the shadowy planets Rahu and Ketu easily take upon
themselves the influence of other planets etc. we have deduced a
corollary from the above rule that in throwing their own malefic
influence on the house these shadowy planets may be aspecting,
they will also throw on the aspected houses the malefic influence
of the malefic planet or planets that may be influencing these
nodes, by association or aspect. For example, if Ketu & Mars are
located in the 6th house in any horoscope or if Ketu is located in
the 6th house & Mars in the 3rd, 11th or 12th house, then Ketu in
throwing its Sth, 7th & 9th aspect will convey to the 10th, 12th & the
2nd houses and will afflict the said houses with the malefic

39

---

## Page 43

influence of Mars as well. This corollary has great impact on the
“Kuja 00572 ` for even though when for example Mars & Ketu are
located together in the 6th house, Mars does not constitute
technically “Kuja 0092 ` in accordance with shloka relating to
this dosha viz.

लग्ने व्यये च पाताले जामित्र चाष्टमे कुजा :

etc. But in actual effect it would shorten the life of the partner very
much because the influence of both Mars & Ketu (killers) would
be felt by the 2nd house which being the longevity (8th) house of
the partner is bound to suffer through the influence of Mars &
Ketu (who also acts like Mars).

भानोस्तु मित्राणि कुजेंदुजीवा : समो बुध : शुक्रशनी विपक्षो ।

इष्टौ शशांकस्य दिनेश सौम्यो शेषा : समा भूमिसुतस्य मित्रम्‌ ।।९३।।
रवीन्दुजीवाश्च बुधश्च शत्रु : समो दिनेशात्मजदानवेज्यौ ।

सौम्यस्य मित्रे दिननाथ शुक्रो शेषासमा रात्रि कर : सपत्न : ।।९४।।
THIN देवगुरो : सपत्नो मित्राणि सर्वे रविजस्तु मध्य
शनीन्दुजाविष्टकरौ मृगोस्तु शेषा : सपत्नाश्च समो FA ।। ९५1
सोरस्य मित्रे भुगुपुत्रसोम्यौ समो गुरुस्ते निखिला : सपत्ना :

राहोस्तु मित्राणि कवीज्यमंदा : केतोस्वथेवात्र वदैति ताज्ञा : ।।९६।।

FRIENDSHIP ETC

The Sun considers Jupiter, Mars and Moon as its friends, It is
neutral towards Mercury. It is inimical to Saturn and Venus.
Moon considers the Sun and Mercury as its friends. It treats the
rest i.e. Saturn, Venus, Jupiter and Mars as a neutral. Mars treats
Sun, Moon & Jupiter as its friends. It is inimically disposed
towards Mercury. It is neutral to Saturn and Venus. Mercury treats
the Sun and Venus as its friends. It is neutral towards Jupiter, Mars
and Saturn, but it is inimical to Moon (94) Jupiter treats Sun, Mars
and Moon as friends, but Venus and Mercury as enemies. Jupiter
is neutral to Saturn. Venus treats Saturn and Mercury as its
friends, It is inimical towards the Sun and the Moon & is neutral
towards Jupiter and Mars (95). Saturn treats Venus and Mercury
as its friends. Jupiter as neutral. While it treats the Sun, Mars and
Moon as its enemies. Rahu treats Venus, Jupiter and Saturn as its
friends. So also is the case with Ketu. (96)

भवैति तात्कालिकमित्रभूता : सर्वे च वाक्सोदरब॑धयुक्ता : ।
स्वात्स्वातक्रमाद्रधुतक्रमतस्तथेवमन्यस्थितास्तत्समयारिभूता : ।।९७।।
तत्कालमित्र तु निसर्गमित्रं दय॑ भवेत्ततत्वधिमित्रसंजञम्‌ ।

तथैव शत्रोरधिशत्नुसंज्ञमेकत्र शत्रु : समतामुपैति ।।९८।।

40

---

## Page 44

Planets located in the 2nd, 3rd or4th house from another planet
orin the 12th, | Ith or 10th from it become temporary friends of the
latter. In other places they become natural enemies. In case the two
are both natural & temporary friends they become Adhimitra i.e.
bosom friends. If both are inimical naturally & temporarily they
become bitter enemies. If friends in one way and enemy in another
they are neutral to each other. (97, 98)

स्वोच्चे सुहृद्भे स्वनवांशेकपि wl दुकाणे दिरसांशकेपि |
कलांशकाद्यशयुतेपि चेवमुपैति तत्स्थानबलं प्रहेन्द्र : ।।९९।।
लगने बुधेज्यौ बलिनो तु पूर्वे वीर्ये यमे तदशेमेर्कभौभौ ।
कामेर्कसूनुर्बलवाञ्जलेशे बंधो निशानाथकवी कुबेरे ।। १००।।
तत्सप्तमे दिग्बलशुन्यमाहुस्तदैतरे चेत्वनुपात एव |
स्वमासहोरादिनवत्सरेषु वीर्यान्विता भानुमुखा प्रहेंद्रा : ।। १०१।।

SIX FOLD STRENGTH
Positional strength

Planets located in their sign of exaltation. in a friendly sign, in
their own Navamsha sign, in the signs they own. in their own
decanteorin 1/12th part, or in their own 1/16th part are considered
to possess “Positional” strength. (99)

DIRECTIONAL STRENGTH

Jupiter and Mercury have full directional strength when located
in the ascendant. Mars & Sun get this full strength when located in
the 10th house, Saturn gets it when located in the 7th house. Moon
and Venus get full directional strength when situated in the 4th
house. Planets are in zero directional strength when located in the
7th house from that where they get full directional strength. In the
intervening situations planets get proportional strength. (100)

TEMPORAL STRENGTH

Sun etc. located in their own month hora, day or year are con-
sidered as strong in temporal strength. (101) i.e. Sun in the Bhadon
month (August and September), Moon in its own hora division”
Mars on Tuesday & Saturn in the year when it is in its own sign,
Capricorn or Aquarius, are considered as strong. (101)

रात्रौ बलादधा शनिकचद्रभोमास्त्रयो ग्रहाश्चाहिन रवीज्यशुक्रा : ।.

सदा बली वित्सितकृष्णपक्षे सौम्यास्तदन्ये बलिन : क्रमेण ।।१०२।।
शुभेक्षिता : पूर्णबलान्वितास्तु दुष्टेर्बलं पापखगेरदृष्ट : ।

सोम्यायने त्वतिबली दिवसाधिनाथ श्चन्द्रस्तदन्यसमये बलपूर्णयुक्त : 1120311

## Page 45

वक्रान्विता : क्षितिसुतप्रमुखा : समस्ता युदरे उयी उलपदिग्गतकांतियुक्त : ।। १०५।।

TIME (KAAL) STRENGTH

Saturn, Moon and Mars get strengthened in a night birth. The
Sun. Jupiter and Venus get strengthened in a day birth. Mercury 15
strong both in day and night births. Benefic planets get strength-
ened in the bright fortnight of the Moon while the malefics get
strengthened in the dark fortnight. (102)

ASPECT STRENGTH ETC.

The planets aspected by benefics and unaspected by malefics are
strong so far as the question of aspect is concerned. The Sun is very
strong in the Uttarain (six months from the Sun's entry into Cap-
ricorn). Moon is strong when the Sun is in Dakshanayan (i.e. in six
months from its entry into Cancer). (103) In natural strength
Saturn, Mars. Mercury. Jupiter, Venus. Moon and Sun are
stronger in order on¢ over the other i.e. Saturn is the least strong &
Sun the most. (104) Planets Mars, Mercury, Jupiter, Venus and
Saturn are strong when in retrogression. A planet is victorious in
war when it has in comparision more northern declination and
has brilliant rays (i.e. are away from the Sun). (105)

Sixfold strength of the Ascendant is as under. (106, 197)

positional strength it is two rupas 3 quarters. in directional

In the sixfold strength Sun gets the maximum strength of six

A planet having a longitude up to the longitude of the house in

दिनमानघटीगुणिता नागहृता गुलिकनाडिका : स्पष्टा : ।।१३३।।
स्फुटगुलिकनाडिकाभिस्तत्कालार्केण सायनेनापि |

तग्नवदानेतव्यो राश्यंशकलादिरूपको गुलिक : ।।१३४।।

GULIK

Al a place where the measure of the day time is 30 ghatis i.e. 12
hours. the Gulik occupies the degree denoted by the Ishta (interval
between the Sun rise & the coming moment of birth) of 26 ghatis
on Sunday. 22 ghatis on Monday 18 ghatis on Tuesday 14 ghatis
on Wednesday 10 ghatis on Thursday, 6 ghatis on Friday & 2
ghatis on Saturday. When the duration of the day is more or less
than 12 hours the Ishta should be ascertained by the rule of 3 i.e. if
on Sunday for 30 ghatis duration it is 26 ghatis. how much is it for
the duration of the day involved. Having ascertained the Gulik
Ishta concerned for the day involved, the Ascendant on that Ishta
worked out in the normal manner gives the Gulik point. (133,
| 34)

चंद्ररुद्र जयवेद्य नृपातोनाखुनाडिनिहिताहि नमानात |
नागलब्धमित्तमांदिघटी स्याल्लग्नवत्स्फुटमिहानयनं हि ५ १३५।।
MANDI

Multiply the measure of the day time by 26, 22, 18. 14, 10, 6 & 2
respectively for the days Sunday to Saturday. Divide the result by

46

---

## Page 50

30, the answer will be the Ishta at which Mandi is. (135)
TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

The author has opined that the product of the duration of the
day period concerned and 26 etc. should be divided by 30. This is
obviously based on the assumption that the duration of the day
would be 30 ghatis which is not the case in most cases. Hence the
appropriate step is to divide the product by the duration of the day
in ghatis instead of by 30 in every case.

पाकेशाद्रसुभात्य शत्रु भवने युक्तोपहारेवरस्तच्छतरर्भवतीह लाभधनमे सोत्थात्मजे
बंधुमे |

भाग्ये वा देशमे समन्वितग्रहस्तच्छोभनाख्यस्तत स्तत्कामान्वित खेचरस्त्वशुभद :
प्रोक्तो ग्रहाणां क्रम : 1123811

If the planet having its sub-period is located in 6th, 8th or 12th, it
is inimical (to some extent) to the planet having the main ruling
period. If located in the rest of the houses except 7th, it acts as a
friend to the dasa lord. The sub-period lord in 7th to the main
period lord gives adverse results. (136)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

The fact that a planet is placed 6th. 8th or 12th from the planet
having its main ruling period makes the sub-period lord adverse
by one point. If it is enemy also of the main period lord it would be
adverse by two points. If it is enemy to the lord of the Ascendant, it
would be adverse by 3 point. If it is located 6th, 8th or 12th from the
lagna it would be adverse by 4 points. If it is placed 6th, 8th & 12th
from the lord of the lagna it would be adverse by 5 points.

Thus a planet that indicates good results in its sub-period by
even 4 points by being in a friendly sign, by owning good houses.
by being in association with a benefic & by being in its Qwn sign
may still give slightly bad results for such a planet is good onlyon 4
counts & bad on 5.

पापग्रहादिसहितो दुचरस्तु शत्रु : स्यात्स्थानतोपि शुभदस्त्वतिशोभनाख्य : ।
स्थानानुरूपफलमेव विचित्य मार्ग ज्ञात्वा वदति मुनयो जगतां सुसिद्धथे ।।१२७।।

The planet having its sub-period. if with a malefic, acts in an
inimical manner. If the Sub-period lord is a good planet in himself
and is also good from the point of view of the house it occupies
from the Main-dasa lord, it gives. very good results. Thus it is
necessary to give the results after due consideration of the position
held by the Sub-period lord from the Main-period lord. (137)

GOOD RESULTS

If a natural benefic planet is lord of any house and is located in
“hat house or aspects it and the houses aspected or associated are
101 under the influence of malefic planets by association or aspec.

he house concerned gets boosted in regard to the traits related to
1. Similarly natural malefic planets. lords of houses similarly
situated do not give nice results. Planets in general are strong when
hey are not in debilitation. eclipsed by Sun or in inimical
signs. (2)

A house that contains its lord, or from whom there are in Sth,
9th, 2nd, 4th, 7th or 10th benefic planets and is not influenced by
malefic planets get strengthened. If reverse is the case the houses
become destroyed. If the yoga is mixed there are mixed results.
This rule is applicable to all houses including the Ascendant.
(5)

A house gets its traits destroyed if its lord is located in the 8th
house, also if it is eclipsed by the Sun, or is in its debilitation sign,
or in an inimical sign or is neither associated with nor aspected by
benefics. In cases where a house contains a planet but that planet
is weak in the manner stated above, even then the traits of the
house get lost. This rule is applicable to all houses including the
Ascendant (6)

SOURCE OF INCOME

Source of income should be declared from the planet occupying
the 10th house from the Ascendant or from the Moon, whichever
is stronger. If the planet occupying is the Sun, the source is father,
if Moon it is mother, if Mars the enemy, if Mercury the source is
the relations, if Jupiter it is from brothers (elder), if Venus it is from
wife. if Saturn the source of income is from servants. The
livelihood is also determined from the nature of the planet who is
lord of the Navamsha sign occupied by the lord of the 10th
house. (7)

ततदभावाद्रध्रपो वा खरेशो द्रेष्काणानां चापि नाथोर्कपुत्र : ।

One dealing with natal or horary Astrology, should declare the

its Main or Sub-ruling period is (a) the lord of the 8th house from

house such as 6th. 8th or 12th or (g) it is Adhi Shatru i.e. bitter
enemy of the lord of the house involved (see shloka 17 of chapter I)
or (h) when that lord is in a sign having no good point in the
Ashtak Varga system, (17 & 18).

धनाधिप : पापखगों यदि स्याच्छन्यारभोगीन्द्रदिनेश्वराणीम्‌ ।

In case the lord of the second house (the House of Wealth) is
having its Main ruling period and there is the Sub ruling period of
any of the planets—Saturn, Mars, Rahul and Sun—then the Sub-
period will give loss of wealth. So also 15 the case, if the second
house contains a malefic planet (20) in the dasa of a malefic
planet lord of the 2nd house & in that of the lord of the sign
occupied by the said malefic lord of the 2nd house. there is loss of
wealth, brought about through the punishment orders of the
Government. There is also at that time relinquishment of position
and opposition from the near and dear ones. (21)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

Shloka nu'nber 20 makes no mention of the influence of the
malefic Sub-period lords on the Main-period lord. It is, therefore.
clear that there is always the influence of the planet having its Sub-
period on the planet having its Main period. This shculd be taken
as a law and applied to all Sub-pcriods 10 get correct results.

(2) The words" तदीश "(78५ Isha) in the opening part of
shloka number 21. go to show that the lord of the sign occupied by
112 lord of any house acts as the latter. This is on the basis of the
theory of dispositorship.

located with the lord of any of houses 6th, 8th or 12th or if the lord
of any one of these bad houses is in lagna one suffers bodily. If,
however, the lord of the lagna is weak but located in a kendra or
rine one does not so suffer. (74) The lord of the sign occupied by
the lord of the lagna is located in any of the bad houses 6th, 8th or
12th gives a weak body. Whatever be the house 1st, 2nd. 3rd etc. if
the lord of the sign occupied by the lord of any house is badly
placed the house suffers in its traits. (75)

(04

## Page 68

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE
It would be seen from shloka number 75 that the dispositors of
the lords ol the various houses act for the traits of the houses con-
cerned. This 15 a very important rule and should never be lost
sight of.

SECOND HOUSE

The following should be studied from the 2nd house :— Those
who are dependent on the native, face. mouth, speech, the right
¢ye. accumulated wealth, education, cating, servants & friends.
(1)

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

It 15 a point for note that the author has opined that education
should be studied and determined from the 2nd house. We are also
of the same opinion and do not consider it advisable to examine
education from 4th or Sth house, ६५ done by some other authors.
The 4tn house relates to desires & as such can give knowledge of
our desired object which may not necessarily be connected with
academic education. The 5th house relates to intelligence & fore
sight rather than to education as such.

The right eye of the younger brother is denoted by the house 2nd
to 3rd i.e. the 4th house. If the 4th house & its lord along with the
Sun suffer at the hands of Saturn & Mars, the younger brother will
have serious trouble in his right eye. Similarly, the 6th house, its
lord & Sun highly afflicted, give serious trouble in the right eye of
the son & so on.

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

A reading of the above shloka shows that the excellence of the
2nd house and its lord indicates support of others by the native. It
may be due to the fact that good usc of accumulated wealth, to
which the 2nd house relates lies in the help of others. It is also
significant to note that the 2nd house of any horoscope is the 11th
house—the house of gains of the masses (4th house) & hence the
people in general gain much through the excellence of their house
of gains.

MATHEMATICS

If Mars is in the 2nd house along with the Moon aspected by
Mercury or with Mercury in kendra, the native understands
mathematics. (36)

If Mercury is the lord of the 2nd house & is in its sign of exalta-
tion, Jupiter is in the Ascendant, and Saturn in the 8th house. the
yoga makes the native a mathematician. (37)

If Jupiter is in kendra or in trine, & Venus is in its sign of ¢xalta-
tion or if the lord of the 2nd house & Mercury are in their 51:15 of
exaltation. the native becomes a mathematician. (38)

If the lord of the 2nd house is Sun or Mars and is aspected by
Jupiter and Venus. & Mercury isin "Paravatamsha™ (see shloka 25
etc of chapter 1) the native knows the rationale of Astrology.
(39)

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

The role of Mercury in making one an Astrologer lies in the fact
that a strong Mercury would give mathematical ability. The
capacity to understand & know the future is given by the
excellence of the 5th house & its lord. for the Sth house relates 10
“future” as distinct from the 9th house which relates to the past
(having crossed the horizon before birth). But to earn from Astro-
logy it would be necessary that there should be an intimate link
between the lagna representing the self of the native & the 5th
house representing the future. A link of Jupiter—the planet that
can 0७१९८७९९ the future with the lagna & its lord would give intuitive
powers to the native. In addition. if the lagna and its lord are in
intimate relation with the 4th & the 12th houses and their lords,
this would be an indication that the native earns from the 4th & the
9th houses i.e. from the personal affairs of the public (4th house) &
their prospects in life (9th from 4th is the 12th house). This is after
all what makes a good Astrologer.

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

Mars like Moon Represents blood. The heavy affliction of Mars
& Moon lead to pollution etc. of blood. For example. if Mars lord
ol the lagna containing Moon or Moon lord of the lagna contain-
ing Mars is afflicted by disease factors such as Saturn and Rahu.

## Page 103

the man gets his blood polluted. If in addition Mercury represent-
ing skin is also afflicted by Saturn or Rahu, the man falls prey to
leprosy. Here is the example of a person who developed leprosy.
Here Moon is lord of lagna occupied by Mars suffring in 8th in the
sign of Saturn & under aspect of Mars. Mars in lagna suffers from
both Saturn & Rahu while Mercury is afflicted by Rahu & Saturn.
Venus in Lagna is no relief as it is dispositor of Saturn.

We give below the horoscope of a person who tried to commit
suicide by taking “sleeping pills” birth date is 28-11-1953. The first

---

## Page 104

point that is relevant to the context is the fact that Moon—the
significator of “Eating” is herself in this case the lord of the house
of cating i.e. the 2nd house. It is obvious that the nature of
influence falling on the 2nd house & on Moon—the lord &
significator of eating would denote the nature of eating. The 2nd
house is fully aspected by Rahu— ua planet that stands tor poison, It
is also aspected by Saturn, another planet representing poison.
Similarly. Moon has on it the surrounding influence of Rihu and
Saturn on one side of it and of Mars & Rahu on the other. Mars too
being a poisonous planet. both the 2nd house. its lord &
significator are under the influence of poisonous planets. Hence
the relevance of poison. It has a case of eating poison as Moon as
the lord and significator of cating 1s involved & not a case of being
bitten by some poisonous reptile etc.

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

Rashmi is the proportional strength of a planet due to its dis-
tance from the point where 1115 in highest debilitation. Suppose we
desire to ascertain the number of Rashmis possessed by the Sun
when its longitude is 11-14-10, Taking out 6-10 from it. the remain-
der 5-4-10 is the distunce of Sun from its highest degree of debilita-
tion. Multiplying 5-4-10 by 7 we get 35-29-10 which divided by 6
gives us 5-29-52 1.0. about 6 Rashmis (for further details sco shloka
| of chapter IV of "Maan Sagari Paddhiti’.

The 6th house being one of cnmity appropriately stands for
“others”. & aliens. Hence the link of the lord or the 6th house with
factors denoting the parents (4th & 9th house) gives alien birth.

relations real as opposed 10 aliens or adopted. While this is true. it

a factor either of realship or of being benetic.

CHAPTER-S
Consideration of 5th & 6th Houses

सुतभवनात्सुतवुद्रिमत्रिणामपि म॑त्रभोजनपितुभावान ।
हृदयोदरप्रवेशं विवेकशक्तिं च निरदिशेन्मतिमान्‌ ।।१।।

The wise should consider the following from the 5th house:—
son, intelligence, ministers, mantra. eating. father. heart. belly.
power of discrimination.

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

1 should be noted that the problems of heart and belly have
been alloted by the author to one and the same house i.e. the Sth.
Thus the 4th house relates to lungs & the Sth mostly to heart & bel-
ly. The lordship of the Sun—the planet representing the heart over
the 51) house-would also suggest that heart's condition should be
considered from the Sth sign & the 5th house.

नाथे : कलत्रात्मजघर्ममानां पुत्रादिचिन्तां कथयेत्स जीवे : ।
बुद्धि तथा सोमसुतात्मजाभ्यां पितुस्तथेवात्मजभाग्यसूर्ये : ।।२।।

SONS

The problems relating to the son should be considered from the
lords of the 7th. 5th & 9th houses & (the significator of the son)
Jupiter. Intelligence from the Sth house (its lord) & Mercury. and
the affairs relating to father from the 5th and 9th house and the
Sun. (2)

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

In regard to the house for the father, it would be observed that
the 9th house has been taken as relating to him and not the 10th as
some would take. The 5th house is relevant to consideration of
affairs relating to the father only on the principle of "Bhavat
Bhavam™ 1.९. Sth being 9th to 9th (the house of father).

पितुर्धनं याति सुखे सभानो पुत्रे शशांके मरण॑ च मातु : ।
सुते शुभे शोभनदृष्टियोगे पुत्रं ददात्येव तदा तदीशे ।।३।।

If the Sun is in the 4th house. the native gets wealth from father.
If Moon is then in the 5th mother dies soon (Moon being very
weak). If a benefic planet occupies the Sth house & is under aspect
of benefic planet & the lord of Sth a benefic. is under aspect of
benefics. the native definitely gets a son. (3)

वंशस्य विच्छेदकर : प्रजातश्चंद्रास्फुजित्यापखगा : क्रमेण ।
खंदारसोख्येषु युतास्तथैव लम्नेश्वरे चंद्रसुतेन युक्तं 113311

FAMILY
A yoga for the discontinuance of the family tree will be con-
stituted if Moon is located in the 10th, Venus in 7th and maletics in
the 4th house and the lord of the lagna is located with
Mercury. (23)
TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

Moon located in the 6th house from any house shortens the lon-
gevity of the relation represented by the house from which itis 6th.
(vide shloka 19 chapter 30 Saravalt). Hence in the case under con-
sideration it being 6th from the house of progeny (5th) would des-
troy progeny. The malcfics (many) located in the 4th house would
have the effect of not only afflicting the Moon located in the 10th
but weakening the longevity of progeny still further. The maleic
square aspect of many malefics on Venus in the 7th house would
also weaken the prospects of progeny.

पापग्रहा रिष्फसुताष्टमस्था वंशस्यविच्छेदकरोऽर्थहीन : ।
निशाकरे लग्नगते सजीवे तत्सप्तमे भूमिसुते शनौ वा ।!२४।।

If malefic planets are located in the 12th, 5th or the 8th house.
the yoga indicates the discontinuace of the family tree & the man
becomes bereft of wealth, If the Moon is in the lagna with Jupiter &
Mars or Saturn is located in the 7th house the results follow.
(24)

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

The location of malefics in the 12th house would deny progeny
as these would afflict the house of longevity (8th) of the progeny.
[he same results would follow by the affliction of the house of pro-
geny (5th). The location of malefics in the 8th house would destroy
the house of “family”,

पापग्रहा ब॑धुगताश्च सर्वे वैशस्य विच्छेदकरोऽन्र जातं : ।
लग्नांत्यपुतराष्टमराशियुक्ते : पापग्रहेंबशविनाशहेतु : ।।२५।।

If all malefic planets are located in the 4th house, the yoga
indicates the discontinuace of the family tree. Similarly, if the
malefic planets occupy the 1st 1211. Sth. 8th houses, then also the
result 15 the same. (25)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

Why the location of all malefic planets in the 4th house destroys
progeny is the question. The answer lies in the principle that the

138

---

## Page 142

heavy affliction of the 12th house leads to the destruction of the
house from whom it is 12th. In this connection please refer to
shloka 1, chapter 8 under 12th house.

15 in lagna, Saturn in 8th. Sun in Sth. (30) but if most of these

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

The 3rd house in the horoscope of any body is the 11th house of
his son i.c. the arms of his son. If the lord of the 3rd house is in the
3rd, it will influence the 9th house—the house of the father in a
dekiberate manner & in case it is a benefice planet it would act to
the advantage of the father. Similarly. if the lord of the 5th house is
in the 4th with strong benefics it will influence the 10th house ie.
the 2nd house or the mouth of the father, which means the son will
feed the father.

TRANSLATORS NOTE

The author has not said much on the question of enemies to

The affliction by malefics of the 6th house and its lord leads to
the creation of enemies. while the question who will win whether
the native or his enemies has to be decided from the fact as to who
15 more strong. If the lagna & its lord are stronger than the 6th
house and its lord the native wins & 11 otherwise is the case, the
encmies win. The aspect of plancts whether benefics or malefics
has to be given more weight than the association of planets. The
horoscope of Shri J.I.. Nchru is an illustration in this context.
His horoscope is as under. The fact that Jupiter in dignity is in

by the Sun (again government). Hence his lifelong struggle against
the British Empire. But the enemy was ultimately defeated due 10
the fact that the lagna & 115 lord Moon are stronger than the 6th

against the British Empire.

house and Sun. should leprosy be declared to the father.. so also to
other relations through their house lords & significators. (7)

The lord of the 6th denotes trouble, Rahu is a planet of separa-

The yoga in our opinion will be more effective if the lord of the
lagna is also afflicted by the lord of the 6th house or by Rahu and
Saturn— planets of dearth & want. for the lord of the lagna would
represent the private organ of wife.

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

When the lords of the 2nd and the 7th are occupying their own
signs in the 2nd and 7th houses respectively, the two houses would
become strong. Since both of these houses stand for the longevity
of wife. the first wife would be long living without necessitating a
second marriage.

The number of planets located with the lords of the 2nd and the
7th houses give the number of wives. The number is also deter-
mined from the number of planets in association with the lord of
the sign occupied by the lord of the 7th house. (14)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE
Mercury in strength is not only a female planct in strength, but
also a factor of plurality in strength. Located in 10th from the lord

163

---

## Page 167

of the lagna Mercury would make the traits of the lagna lord plural
as it would throw its 3/4th aspect on it. Since the lagna is 7th to 7th,
it represents 7th 1.९. wife & hence wife would be made plural by the
said yoga. Similarly Moon is also a female planet like Mercury in
10th (upchaya) Moon would also be in an upchaya house trom the
lord of the 7th & would denote gain of wives. For the relevince of
upchaya houses to the problem of many wives see also shloka 30 &

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

The 12th house stands for विवाह. according to the dictum
" (था भोग विवाहेषु ". The 2nd also denotes marriage according to
Maharshi Parashar vide shloka 9 chapter 22 bphs. Hence when
the lords of these houses are located in the 3rd house—an upchaya
(gain) house. the yoga would denote much gain of wives par-
ticularly when aspected by the best of benefics 1.९. Jupiter & the
priest for marriage & by another best of planets viz the lord of the
9th house. It would also be noted that the 3rd house 15 2nd to 2nd
and 4th 10 12th re. very well placed from both. For this reason too
the prospects of the 12th and the 2nd (marriage) would prosper.

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

One of the conditions for the loyality of the wife laid down is
that the lord of the 7th house should be a friend of the lord of the
lagna. This is generally not so as the two planets involved in the
case of every Ascendant are mutually inimical. What is probably
meant is that the lord of the 7th house should be a temporary
friend of the lord of the lagna (sec shloka 97 of chapter 1).

or in the highest degree of its exaltation, the wife comes from a very

to Saturn, lord of the lagna, (native) who is classed as most inferior
in scale.

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTE

The idea behind the method stated in shloka 77 for finding out
the lagna of the wife is to find out the predominating influence on
the factors that represent wife. Since under the fundamental prin-
ciple of astrology all problems have to be tackled by a considera-
tion of the house concerned. its lord and the significator involved,
we think we should determine the dominant planet & its sign that
influence the 3 fundamental factors. We suggest our own horos-
cope as an illustration. We will tackle the problem of the sign of
our younger & ¢lder brother.

PE

2 „>

Sign in the 3rd house is Virgo. This 3rd house, its lord and Mars
the significator of younger brothers have to be taken as the basic
influenced factors. Virgo or the sign of Saturn may be the brothers
sign, the lord of 3rd Mercury is influenced by Jupiter, Sun, Mars &
Venus. It may give a sign belonging to any one of these. The
significator Mars is influenced by Sun, Mercury, Jupiter and
Venus. It may give the sign of any of these. Since Mercury is
involved in all the three cases & is thus dominant, the younger
brother should be born with Virgo as his Ascendant, which is
actually the case. Similarly in the case of elder brother the sign in

174

---

## Page 178

the 11th house, Moon & Saturn aspecting it, Leo in which the
significator of elder brothers viz Jupiter is situated or Venus who is
influencing Jupiter through the 9th aspect of Ketu aspected by
Venus may give their sign. Since Venus has the predominent
influence on the relevant factors, Taurus—the sign of Venus in the
I 1th house—wins. Hence Taurus is the lagna of the elder brother
which is actually the case.

from 32 to 69. it is middle and beyond 69 it is called “long”

15 long. one lives till middle age if the lord of the lagna 15 weak,

It would be noted that the 6th house 15 one of injury. Its lord is

lord of the sign occupied by Ketu & then you have an idea of how
injurious Mars can prove. It can give death by injury if it influen-
ces the factors stated at the beginning of this note. Here if you
know that according to Maharshi Parashar Rahu aspects 1.६.
influences the house located 9th from it you will see that the 8th
house of the birth chart. showing manner of death is influcnced by

planet associated with it, 11 throws on the 8th house the killing &
injury influence of Mars thereby showing death by injury. The
influence of Mars is felt on each side of the !st house & the house
containg Mercury. the lord of the 8th house. Thus the influence of
Mars & Ketu is falling on all factors denoting mode of death. Since
Mars is lord of the 10th & 3rd houses from the 4th, it brought about
death by the deliberate action of some member of the public
denoted by the 4th house.

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE
The mode of death is indicated by the nature of influence falling
on the 151 & 8th house or their lords. In the case under considera-
tion the influencing planets arc Mars & the lord of the 6th house,
each of which is an injury planet. Hence death through injury by
weapons represented by Mars.

ACTIONS

If the lord of the 10th house is weak and under the influence of
malefics. the yoga indicates frustrations in actions. When the lord
of the 10th house. Jupiter and Mercury are strong the native is
engaged in the service of others. (2)

These three planets. when strong and aspected by natural
benefics. make the native particularly engage himself in acts of
helping public causes. If. however, these are in 6th. 8th. or 12th
house. badly aspected. there is absence of such acts. (3)

114 plancts are together in any place other than a kendra and if

11 Sun occupies the decante of Saturn and is aspected by Saturn.

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

The rationale behind the Sanyas yoga constituted by the loca-
ion together of 4 planets in a kendra is not quite clear. From a

206

---

## Page 210

perusal of the texts it is thought that according to the texts the loca-
tion of planets in a kendra or trinal house influences the Ascen-
dant. Based on this principle the location of 4 planets in any
kendra would have the influence of the four planets on the lagna.
Since the association of 4 planets is generally of a “"Separative”
character in view of the inclusion of one or more of the seperative
planets. Sun. Saturn, ९२२1५. Mandi. etc the influence of the 4
planets gathered together in a kendra will be one of separation on
the lagna which will have the effect of separating one from the
traits of the Ist house, viz wealth and th: place of birth, there is
some justification in the yoga in question.

(2) We. however. think that it would be better if we have a defini-
tion of the term “Sanyas™ & consider the question from the
astrological factors involved. Sanyas in our opinion is formed
when the mind 15 in Vairagya and the native leaves his family,
home and wealth & cnjoyments of the bed. This will be there if
Moon. the 4th house and its lord. representing the mind are under
the influence of the significator of Sanyas-Saturn & Rahu who
always acts as Saturn. This will suffice to give the requisite
Vairagya. Then the influence of the “Scparative”™ planets. Sun.
Saturn and Rahu or their dispositors should be on the 2nd house
and its lord (family) on the 4th house and its lord (Residence) & on
the 12th house and its lord (pleasures of the bed).

(3) In actual life we can verily the correctness of the above state-
ment. We will present some illustrative horoscopes. The birth
chart of Shri Chaitanya is given below. See the intensity of

SSC

Vairagya given by the 10th aspect of Saturn on Moon—the
significator of mind. See the full 8th aspect of Mars—the dis-
positor of Saturn on Moon. Sce the location of Saturn in the 4th
house from Moon. Sce the aspect of Saturn on the lord of the 4th
house from Moon. Sce the aspect of Saturn on the 4th house
from lagna.

Navamsha. (3)

CHAPTER 9
RAJ YOGAS

षटभिर््रहेरुच्वसमन्विते : स्याद्राजाधिरा जो बहुदेशभर्ता |
उच्वस्थिते : पत्चभिरत्र राजा शक्तयान्वितो देवगुरौ विलग्ने 1 1१ ।

कुम्मे विलग्ने भृगुन॑दने वा स्वोच्चस्थिते भूमिपतिश्चतुर्भि : ।
उच्चस्थितेनीचवियुक्तमागे : त्रूरादिषष्टय॑शविहीनभागै : ।।२।।

If in any birth chart there are planets occupying their sign of
cxaltation, the native becomes a king of kings. ruler over many
territories. If there are only five planets in exaltation and there is
Jupiter in strength in the Ascendant, the native becomes a king. (1)
If the Ascendant is Aquarius and Venus is in exaltation & there are
in all four planets in exaltation, but are not occupying any
debilitation Navamsha or cruel 1/60th part of the sign even then
the native becomes a king. (2)

लग्ने वृषे तंत्र गते शशांके षड़भिर्गहिरुच्चगतैरनप : स्यात्‌ ।
कस्मिन्‌ गृहे स्वोच्चयुते तु सवे : स्वक्षेत्रैर्भूपतितुल्यजात : ।।३।।

मूलत्रिकोणांकितराशियुक्तैमितर्षगैर्वा यदि वक्रयुक्तै : ।
कस्मिन्‌ गृहे स्वोच्वयुतेत्र शेषेनीचांशडीनेनूपतुल्यजात : ।।४।।

जनयति नृपमेकोप्युख्वगो मित्रदृष्ट : प्रचुरधनसमेतं मित्रयोगाच्च सिद्रम्‌ ।
विवसुविसुखमूटव्याधितं ब॑धतप्ते वधदुरितसमेतं शत्रुनिम्नर््षणेषु ।।५।।

If Moon occupies its sign of exaltation in the Ascendant and
there are in all 6 planets in exaltation, the native becomes a king. If
all planets are occupying their sign of ¢xaltation anywhere in the
horoscope. then also the native becomes a king. In case all the
planets are located in their own signs the native though not a king
is equal in status to a king. (3)

13 planets occupy their Mool Trikona signs or if 3 planets are in
friendly signs in retrogression and the rest are located in exaltation
without occupying their debilitation Navamsha the native has
status equal to that of a king. (4)

Even a single planet located in exaltation aspected Ly its friend.
makes the native a king having much wealth—and succesful due
to cooperation of his friends. On the other hand. if many planets
are occupying inimical or debilitation signs the native becomes

devoid of wealth. and comforts: foolish, discased. with no Ireedom

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

From a perusal of shloka 4 above it would be seen that a planet
occupying a friendly sign and in retrogression is almost equal to
an exalted planct 11 not beter. Retrogression is thus always a sign
of strength.

also from cach (<+, they are said to constitute karaka yoga.

It 15 casy to understand that a planet in its own sign &

voga. the influence of exalted planets mutually boosts still further
their strength and thereby leads to affluence & power.

DESTRUCTION OF GOOD YOGAS

जीवे सकेतौ यदि वा सराहौ वाण्डालता पापनिरीक्षिते वेत्‌ ।

If Jupiter is with Rahu or Ketu & is aspected by a malefic planet,
it creates "(1211081 yoga i.e. a yoga denoting bad character of the
native. Similarly, if Jupiter is located with a planet in its sign of

tion, the same result follows even if the man is a Brahmin. (1)

वंध्यास्त्रिया : संगमनं रवौ स्यान्मैदे शशांके भवने समानम्‌ ।
रजस्वलासंगमनं कुजे तु वंध्यांगनासंगमन॑ च वाच्यम्‌ ।।५४।।

बुधे तु वेश्यागमनं मदस्थे हीनांगनासंगमनं वणिग्जा ।
मदे गुरो ब्राह्मणमार्यया वौ मृगौ तु गर्मान्वितभामिनी वा ।।५५।।

सपुष्पिणी जातिविहीनिका वा गम्या भवेत्तेन शनिध्वजाद्य : ।
राहौ मदे गर्भिणिसंगम : स्यात्कृष्णा च कुष्जा शशिना वदति ।।५६।।

If Sun is in the 7th house one cohabits with a stirile woman. if
Sun 15 there in the sign of Moon, the cohabitation is with a woman
of equal qualification. If it is Mars the sexual act is with a woman
in menses or with a stirile woman. If Mercury is there in the 7th
house it indicates prostitution or with a woman of low status or
one belonging to the trader class. If Jupiter is in the 7th the act is
with a Brahmin woman. If it is Venus the act is with a pregnant
woman. (54-55)

If it is Saturn, Ketu etc the act is with a pregnant woman or a
woman of low caste. If it 15 Rahu in the 7th house the sexual act is
with a pregnant woman. If it 1४ Moon the act is with a dark & bent
up woman. (These results follow if the planets are in their debilita-
tion signs or in inimical sign.) (56)

सुखस्थितैरीदृशसंगमस्तु वाच्यस्तदा व्योमचरेविंशेषात्‌ |
सूर्यादिभिव्योमयर : सुखस्थर्वाच्या तयो : संगमनस्य शाला ।।५७।।

Such type of sexual acts should also be declared by planets in
the 4th house. By Sun etc in the 4th house the type of tiic house
used for the act should be determined. (57)

वनं गृहं शुन्यगृह विहारस्थानं तु देवालयतोयभूमि : ।

If it is Sun in the 4th the act is in a jungle; if Moon. it is in the
house; if Mars, it is in an uninhabited house; if it is Mercury. itis a
pleasure resort; if it is Jupiter, it is in a temple; if it is Venus, it is
near watery place; if it is Saturn, in a fort or in a place reclaimed as
watery place. (58)

केन्द्रे चतुष्के यदि पापयुक्ते जात: पशुनां मिधुनं समेति ।
केन्द्रेत्रिके पापयु्त यदि स्यात्पश्वादिवन्मैथुनमेति जात : ।\५९।।

It all the four kendras are occupied by malefic planets, the
nativs has the sexual act with animals. If only three of the kendras
arc occupied by malefics, tli¢ native performs the sexual act like an

कुशस्तना भूमिसुते मदस्थे ल॑वस्तना मंदफणीद्रकेतौ |
काठिन्यतश्चोर्ध्वकुचा रवौ स्याच्छेषग्रहैरु्तमकोमलीगी । 15011

If Mars occupies the 7th house the woman has very small sized
breasts. If Saturn, Rahu or Ketu is in the 7th she has long breasts. If
Sun is there the breasts are hard. If any one of the rest are there in
the 7th house the woman. has very nice & soft limbs. (60)

चन्द्रे कृशांगे परि जीर्णगेहं तस्मिन्बलि.ठ ge नवीनम्‌ |
दुःस्थे यदि स्याच्छनिराहुकेतौ दाहेन तप्तं नियमेन काच्यम्‌ ।।६१।।

If Moon in the 4th house is within 72 degrees from the Sun. the
house is old. If she 15 strong the house is new and pucca. If Saturn,
Rahu and Ketu are in the 6th, 8th or 12th the house remains in
heated condition. (61)

धनायपो लग्नपतेस्तु मित्र धनं तदीयं द्विजदेवतार्थम्‌ 11811
