केचिद्योगं प्रशंसन्ति दशां केचिद्वदन्ति हि ।
gle चायुष॑ ज्ञातुं न शक्य॑ तु मनीषिभि : ।।१।।

SPAN OF LIFE

Some authors praise the Yogas in astrology; others the Dasa
System. They say Dasa System of ruling periods is important for
without it even the learned are unable to tell any thing about the
span of life. (1)

त्रिविघाश्चायुष्षं योगा : स्वल्यायुर्मध्यमोत्तमा : |
हत्रिशत्पूर्वमल्यं स्यात्तदुषव मध्यमं भवेत्‌ ।।२।।

आसप्ततेस्तदुर्ध्व तु दीर्घायुरिति संमतम्‌ |
उत्तमायु : शतादुर्ध्वमिह शंसन्ति तद्विद : ।।३।।
There are 3 kinds of yogas of longevity: less than 32 years 15
called short one—from 32 to 70 it is medium & above 70 it is

declared as long. The longevity over 100 years is termed as "पगा `
or the highest. (2 & 3)

आद्रादशाब्दा ज्ज॑तुनामायुर्ञातुं न शक्यते |
जपहोमचिकित्सादयेर्बालरक्षां तु कारयेत्‌ ।।४।।

It is not possible to assess the longevity of people till they are of
12 years of age. Upto 12 the life of the young ones should be looked
after by Japa, oblations, & medical prescriptions. (4)

पिन्नोदेषिर्मुता : केचित्केचिद्मालग्रहैरपि ।
अपरे रिष्टयोगाच्च त्रिविधा बालमृत्यव : ।।५।।

Some children die before 12 as a result of the fault of their
parents. Some die of cruel planets governing the early age, others
dic of yogas causing early death. Thus there are 3 types of deaths of
young children. (5)

जन्मत : प्रबलेनैव बालानां पुष्टिवर्दनम्‌ |
कथयेदेव शेषं तु तत्तद्योगानुरूपत : 11511
The sound health of children should be seen from the strong

planets in their birth charts. The rest should be declared on the
basis of yogas. (6)

## Page 241

अल्पीयुर्तीग्नपं भानां : शत्री मध्ये तु मध्यमम्‌ ।
मित्रे लग्नेश्वरे तस्य दीर्धमायुरुदाहृतम्‌ ।।७।।

If the lord of the lagna is enemy of the Sun, one gets short life. If
it is neutral, the span of life is also medium. If it is friendly, the
span is long. (7)

अल्पायुर्योगजातस्य विपद्दाये मृतिम्वदेत्‌ ।
जतस्य मध्यमे योगे प्रत्यरौ तु मृतिवदेत्‌ ।।८।।

For people born in yogas giving only short life (see shlokas 2 & 3
anti) death takes place in the dasa of the planet governing the
Vipat star (3rd from the tenth star). For those born with medium
life it takes place in the “Pratyari™ dasa. (8)

वीर्घायुर्योगजातानां वघभे तु मृति वदेत्‌ ।
जाटस्य मध्यमे योगे प्रत्येकं त्रिविघ॑ भवेत्‌ ।।९।।

People having long span of life die in the dasa of the planet
governing the “Vadha" star (7th from that of birth). (9)

चरस्थिरेति सूत्रेण दीर्घमध्याल्पकायुष : |
तयोदन्यतमं ज्ञात्वा चायुर्ान प्रचक्षते ।। १०।।

The range of longevity should be determined by the use of the
rule relating to the 3 types of signs i.e. movable, fixed and common.
(10)

TRANSLATOR’'S NOTE

The shloka refers to the sutras of Jaimini. According to Jemini
the signs occupied by the lords of the lagna & that of the 8th house
should be secn. If both the planets are located in a movable sign (1,
4,7, or 10) the native will have "long" life. Also when one of them is
in a fixed sign and the other in a common one.

If both the planets are located in a fixed sign (2, 5. 8. or 11) the
native gets “short” life; also when one of them is located in 2 mov-
able sign & the other in a common one.

If both of them occupy a common sign (3, 6, 9, or 12) the native
gets “medium” life span. So also if one of the planets occupies a
movable sign and the other a fixed one.

अल्पायूरल्पमध्यं तु पूर्णायुस्त्रिविधं स्मृतम्‌ ।
मध्यमादल्पमध्यं तु पूर्णायुस्त्रिविधं भवेत्‌ ।।११।।

The short life is divided into three parts i.e. short, medium &
highest. Similarly we have short, medium & highest, in the
medium range. (11)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

How the weakness of the lagna and its lord leads to short life is
illustrated by the horoscope of late Shri Surya Prakash, son of Shri
B.V. Raman of the Astrological Magazine, Bangalore. Here the

cury the dispositor of malefic Ketu. Moon too standing as one of
the lagnas is weak in “Paksha™ strength, being within 72 degrees
from the Sun & its dispositor. Jupiter afflicted by the 10th aspect of
Saturn. The weakness of the lagnas, apart from other defects, led
primarily to death at the age of 28.

What is one man’s food is another man's poison. The rules

be shunned. In the world periods denoting turns of roads. seasons,

that period is dangerous to the life of the native.

within 7 years. (39)

by Saturn surely kills the newly born within 4 years of its birth.

is weak in paksha strength is located within 72 degrees from the
Sun. & is aspected by all malefics & by none of the benefics. kills
the native within 3 years of its birth. (61)

पापो विलग्नाधिपति : शशांकादैत्यस्थित : क्रूरनिरीक्षितरचेत्‌ ।

CHAPTER—11
Cancellation of yogas for short life.

CHAPTER—12
MEDIUM LONGEVITY
द्वात्रिशदुर्ध्वमर्वक्त : सप्तत्या मध्यमायुर्योगान्‌ |
तावत्कालनियमितान्‌ योगविशेषानहं वक्ष्ये ।।१।।

I will now deal with yogas relating to medium longevity i.e. from

33 to 70 years of age. (1)

संज्ञाघ्याये यस्य यदु्रश्यभक्तं कर्माजीवे यस्य यच्चोपदिष्टम्‌ |

The results of a ruling period should be declared by taking into
account all objects etc that are relavant to the planet in the chapter
of definitions & in that dealing with profession, as also by the
thing relating to the house involved, the aspect falling on it, or the
yoga made with it. (35)

सूर्य स्थानबलाधिके कृषिघन॑ गोभूमियानांबरं सौख्यं राजसुमाननं परघनै : संयुज्यते
कांतिमान्‌ |

महत्‌ ।1३६।।

When the Sun is strong by possessing the strength arising out of
the place (sce shloka 99 to 100 of chapter 1) it gives in its ruling
period agricultural wealth, cows. land, conveyance, clothes. com-
forts, honour from the government, wealth from others, lustre of
the body. In the ruling period of the Sun one gets articles for sleep
(good bed etc) and clothes. One also engages himself in the great
service of others, & dips in the sacred waters accompanied by
fame, ornaments, & the aquisition of good friends & relatives.
(36)

रवौ यदा स्थानबलेन हीने तत्पककाले बलमर्थनाशम |
स्थानच्युतं ब॑धुविरोघतापं देशादिदेशं समुपैति दुःखम्‌ 11391

He falls from the position held. there is opposition from friends
and relatives. mental worry & sorrow by thoving from place to

दिग्वीर्ययुक्ते दिवसेश्वरे तु दिर्गतराक्रात धनोपि सौख्यम्‌ |

During the ruling period when the Sun is endowed with dirce-

nol get such intensive results if the Sun has good strength but not

strength. one gets gain from agriculture, lands. wealth. He gets suc-

During the ruling period of the Sun endowed with the strength

During the ruling period of Sun when it is located in a malefic

loss of father 516 or his own destruction. (43)

During the ruling period of Sun located in the Navamsha of its

MAIN RULING PERIOD OF MOON

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

When a planet is dispositor of malefic planets it acts as a malefic
planetin its ruling or subperiod. The point would be clear from the
following horoscope of the translator. Even though both Venus

कै

">€

and Moon are watery planets, the face of the translater caught fire
from an inflammable material on 12-1-1925 when he was having
the main ruling period of Venus and the sub ruling period of Moon.

283

---

## Page 287

The reason must be looked for in the fact that Moon is the dis-
positor of 3 firy planets viz Sun, Mars & Mercury & by aspecting
Taurus (face) it threw the fire on the face & on Venus the main
period lord who is always influenced by the sub period lord.

च॑द्रदशायामादौ नरपतिसन्मान कीर्तिसोख्यं च ।

CHAPTER—14
MARS

अत्युच्वभून॑दनदायकाले क्षेत्राथलाभ॑ समरे जयं च |
अधिक्यमन्वेति नरेशमान॑ सहोदरस्त्रीसुतवाग्विलासम ।।१।।

During the ruling period of Mars located in its highest degree of
exaltation, the native gets lands, wealth, victory in battle. much
honour from the government, also comforts of brothers, wife, son.
& enjoyment of speech. (1)

उच्च॑गतस्य च दशासम्ये कुजस्य प्राप्नोति राज्यमथवा क्ितिपाच्चवित्तम्‌ ।
भूमध्यदारसुतब॑धुसमागमं च यानादिरोहणविशेषविदेशयानम ।।२।।

During the ruling period of Mars located in its sign of exalta-
tion, the native gets ruling powers or wealth from government,
inflow of lands. wife, son, relatives and friends, honour, special
conveyance, & foreign travel. (2)

आरोहिणी भूमिसुतस्य सौख्यं दशा तनोत्यत्र नरेन्दरपूज्यम्‌ |
प्रधानतां धेर्यमनोपिलाष॑ं भाग्योत्तरं गोगजवाजिस॑घम्‌ 11311

During the ruling period of Mars located in the sign previous to
that of its exaltation, the native gets comforts, favour from govern-
ment getting into prominence. he gets patience. cherished object
rise in prospects & gets cattle such as cows. clephants &
horses. (2)

धरासुतस्याप्यवरोह काले स्थानार्थनांशं कलिकोपदुः खं |
विदेशवासं स्वजनेर्विरोघं चोराग्निभूपैर्भयमेति कष्टम्‌ ।।४।।

During the ruling period of Mars occupying a sign previous to
its sigr. of debililation. there is loss of property. wealth. rifl. anger
and sorrow, abode in a foreign land. opposition to onc’'s own peo-
ple. & fear & trouble from thieves. fire & the ruler. (4)

नीचस्थितंस्यापि धरासुतस्य दाये कुवत्या स्वजनादिरक्ा |
कुभोजन गोगजवाजिनाशं स्वेबन्धुनाशं नृपवहनिचौर : ।।५।।

During the ruling period of Mars located in its sign of debilita-
tion (Cancer) the native protects his people by bad means. takes
bad food. there is loss to him of cattle, such as cows. & horses. loss
of relatives & losses through the ruler. thieves and fire. (5)

शुभेक्षितघरासुनोदयि भृम्यर्थनाशनम्‌ |

TRANSLATOR'’S NOTES

It seems the word, शुभ has been used in this shloka instead of
" अशुभ ` 0८10९ results for शुभ effect have already been stated in
the previous shloka. We have therefore given the results arising
out of malefic aspect on Mars.

(2) The word गोचर (Gochar) used in the shloka has not been
used in any sense of transit. A Gochar planet is one which is strong
& well aspected & without any bad influence. “Agochar” is one
which is weak, badly influenced, without any good influence
etc.

भारस्य पापग्रहवीछिंतस्य प्राप्तौ दशायां बहुदुः खकष्टं |
जन : परित्यक्तकलन्रामत्रो देशांतरस्थ : श्ितिपालकोपात्‌ ।।१८।।

During the ruling period of Mars aspected by malefic planet, the
native gets much sorrow & trouble. He is forsaken by people, his
wife & friends, & he has to live in another territory as a result of
wrath of the ruler. (18)

केद्रगतभोमदाये चोरविषाभ्यामुपैति दुः खाति |
कलहो वा स विरोधं लभते देशांतरं याति ।।१९।।

During the ruling period of Mars occupying a kendra, the native
suffers from thieves. poison; he gets into clashes with others and
gets loss of peace of mind & has to travel to another country.
(19)

चतुर्थ राशिस्थित भौमदाये स्थान च्युतिं बंधुविरोधतां च ।
चौराग्निपीडां नृपते : सकाशादभीति परे दुर्गपदे प्रयाति 11011
During the ruling period of Mars occupying the 4th house, the
native has to leave his residence. gets opposition from his friends
and relatives. He gets trouble froin the ruler. & trouble from
thieves and fire and has to perform very difficult tasks. (20)

अगोचरस्थस्य च तादुरौव तदन्यथा चेत्फलमन्यथैव ।।२१।।

MAIN RULING PERIOD OF MERCURY

अत्युल्वसोमात्मजदायकाले धनान्वित : ख्यातिमुपैति सौख्यम्‌ ।
ज्ञान च कीर्तिं जननायकत्वं स्त्रीपुत्रभूम्यर्थ महोत्सवं च ।। १।।

During the ruling period of Mercury located in the highest
degree of exaltation (viz the 15 degree of Virgo) the native gets
wealth, comforts and fame, wisdom, leadership over others, happi-
ness from wife, son, lands, & wealth. (1)

उच्वस्थितस्यापि शशांकसूनोदशा महत्वं कुरुतेर्थसोख्यम्‌ |

During the ruling period of Mercury located in its sign of exalta-
tion, the native gets high position, wealth and comfcrts, strength of
body, grains, sons, cows, horses, elephants and the music of the
instrument “Mridanga”. (2)

आरोहिणी सौम्यदशा प्रपन्ना यज्ञोत्सवं गोवृषवा जिसंघम ।

During the ruling period of Mercury occupying its sign prior to
that of exaltation, the native gets celebration of yagya. cows. oxen,

horses, nice food, ornaments, ciothes, honour, gain from trade.
lands & there are acts of service of others. (3)

Gandhi).

CHAPTER-—15
RULING PERIOD OF JUPITER

गुरोदशायां परमोच्वगस्य राज्यं महत्सोख्यमुपेति कीर्तिम्‌ |

During the ruling period of Jupiter located in its highest degree
of exaltation, the native gets ruling powers, much happiness &
fame. comforts, elephants & horses. honour from the ruler & rul-
ing over ones own people. (1)

कुलीरगस्यापि गुरोदशायां भाग्योत्तरं भूपतिमाननाद्वा |
विदेशयानं महदाधिपत्यं दुःख : परिकिलन्नतनुर्मनुष्य : ।।२।।

During the ruling period of Jupiter located in Cancer, the native
gets up in prospects, & is honoured by the government. He goes
abroad. & gets ruling powers but is afflicted with sorrow. (2)

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

Sorrow would result if Jupiter is afflicted. Jupiter is considered
in Astrology as the best of benefics, which no doubt it is. But in
actual experience it has sometime, though not always failed to act
as the benefic planet. We would like to give an example. Here is the
birth chart of a boy from the family of the translator of this work.
The native died in his 7th or 8th year of life. inspite of its full 5th

ण XE

DC ह

aspect on lagna. Jupiter 15 not only in exaltation but is also in
retrogression & therefore, should be considered as strong. Then
Moon is full. There must be some reason for short life. We do not
subscribe to the view that a planet in exaltation but in retrogres-
sion acts as a debilitation planet. Here Jupiter is no doubt weak but

305

---

## Page 309

not for being in retrogression while in exaltation. The reason lies
"in the fact that Jupiler is fully aspected by an extra malefic Saturn.
Saturn aspecting Jupiter was not sufficient to turn Jupiter from a
benefic to a malefic but when you consider the fact that Saturn is
the dispositor of as many as 3 malefics viz Sun. Mars & Mercury
you can al once see the malefic influence of 4 planets on Jupiter.
Jupiter is also fully aspected by the Sth aspect of Rahu who in
doing so throws on Jupiter the extremely malefic influence of
Saturn. You can thus see Jupiter is under not less then 8 malefic
influences. In the circumstances Jupiter is out & out a malefic
planet harming the life prospects by aspecting the lagna! Strange
but true for the reasons stated above Moon the dispositor of the
71४16116 Jupiter is acting as a malefic planet & harming Mercury,
the lord of the house of longevity. (8th)
आरोहिणी देवगुरोर्महत्व दशा प्रपन्ना कुरूतेर्थभूमिम्‌ |

During the sub period of the planet located in the 4th house from

other hand even a benefic planet located 4th from the planet hav-

a position of strength, such as its own sign or its sign of exaltation.

etc if the planet in the sub period is natural benefic. If otherwise in

During the main ruling period of the Sun located in the Ascen-
dant and the sub periods of Mars. Saturn. Ketu and Rahu the
native gets sorrow & loss of ruling powers. wealth and property. (1)
This would be the result when the planets Mars etc are in
“Agochar™ position ie. are ill placed from the Sun & weak. If
however, they are in" Gochar™ they give good results. (2) A planet
in its own sign, in its sign of exaltation. in its friends sign. not eclip-

technically called in gochar. (3) If it is eclipsed in debilitation sign.
and in sign other than its Mool Trikon sign or other than a friends
sign & when located in 6th. 8th or 12th house 15 bad and 15
technically called “Yam gochar™. (4)

During the main ruling period of the Sun located in the Ascen-
dant and in the sub periods of Jupiter. Venus, Moon or Mercury.
the native gets benefitted from agriculture. cows, sons, wile and
lands. (5)

During the ruling period of the Sun located in the 2nd house
and in the sub period of malefics there will be loss of wealth, use of
curt speech. mental sorrow, eye disease, & great trouble. (6) During
the main ruling period of the Sun located in the 2nd house and in
the sub period of benelic planets there will be much comfort.
acquisition of education, favour from government, and gain of
clothes. conveyance. (7) During the main ruling period of the Sun
Iocated in the 3rd house and in the sub period of malefics who are
"Gochar Sthan™ 1.e. well placed and strong the native gets much
comfort; If the planets having sub period are not *Gochar Sthan™
the results are bad 1.९. sorrow etc. (8)

TRANSLATOR'S NOTE

There are a few points to be specially noted about the above opi-
nion of the author. In the first place (vide shloka 7) it must be
remembered that academic education & its extent and quality
have 10 be determined from the 2nd house of the horoscope i.e.
through the nature of influence falling on the second house & its
lord and its significator (Mercury). Such education is not to be
scen from any other house such as the 4th and the Sth as some peo-
ple do. Secondly, it would be seen that a uniform principle runs
through the method of prediction taught by the author. The princi-
ple is that the planet. whether a natural malefic or a natural
benefic. must be taken as influencing the planet having its main
ruling period irrespective of the house occupied by them.

In that event. the sub period of Mars located any where will
harm the right eye. if sun in the 2nd house is having its main ruling
period. In case. where Mars is strong and aspecting also the Sun in
the 2nd house, injury to the right eye is a certainty. The reason is
that Mars in such a case will have double malefic influence on the
factors representing the right eye viz the 2nd house and the
planet Sun.

As regards the "Gochar sthan™ position of the planets having
their sub period. we are of the opinion that the benefit or harm to

340

---

## Page 344

the house occupied by the main dasa lord would be much when
the planets having their sub periods are strong. for then their
influence. good or bad. will be more effective.

In the text the shloka for the results of the sub periods of the
benefic planets in the main period of Mars located in the 10th
house 15 missing. Following the trend of the method of deliniation
by the author it may be stated that the results of such sub periods
should give honour to the native, good actions on his part. and suc-
cess in action but bad name and adverse results at the end of the
sub period.

SUB PERIODS IN DASA OF SATURN

केन्द्रस्थस्य शनेर्दयि यदा पाप ERE |

फलमीदुशमादौ तु भुक्तयंते रोगपीडनम्‌ ।

During the sub period of malefic planets in the main dasa of
Saturn located in kendra the native falls from his position in life.
He has to live in a different place and suffer through government,
thieves and fire. (1)

During the sub periods of benefics, however, he gets much hap-
piness. honour from government. wealth, and rule over the coun-
try or a village. (2) Such is the result during the first half of the
benefic sub periods. At the end of the sub periods the native gets
disease. bad name, death of relatives. and loss of wealth. (3)

यंदथ्यज्जन्मनि नक्षत्रे वृद्धिमावमुपेयुषि ।
तस्य श्रीरायुरारोग्य॑ भवत्येवं विनिश्चय : ।।१।।

तिथ्यादिषु तथा वाच्यं क्षये तस्मिन्‌ कयो भवेत्‌ ।
तिथिरेकगुणा प्रोक्ता तक्षं दशगुणं भवेत्‌ ।
लग्न लक्षगुणं प्रोक्तं तत्समूहे कलादिकम्‌ ।।२।।

In horoscopes where the nakshatra (asterism) is of increased
duration i.e. where it last for 24 hours on the previous day and
extends to the next day as well, the native gets health, wealth etc.
Similar good results should be declared where tithi (lunar date) etc
also extends similarly. (1)

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

In case the tithi etc is of kshaya type with two lunar dates end in
a particular date & some part of the 3rd lunar date also starts in
that day, the lunar date coming in the middle of the 3 lunar dates is
termed as “Kshaya" tithi. It is taken as a malefic tithi.

The longevity etc is short accordingly. The tithi may be keptasa
unit, the asterism is tenfold in results & the lagna lakh times more.
The integrated results should be taken. (2)

केन्दरस्थिता जन्मनि यस्य कस्य पापाश्च सर्वे वरिफलप्रवा : स्यु : ।

पापग्रहे कर्मगतेति नीचे वक्रान्विते पापखगै : प्रवृष्टे ।
नाशं कलत्रस्य वदति नून मुनीश्वरास्तददनेकशास्त्रे : ।।४।।

दुःखी मूढो लोकक्दिषकारी काण : पंगुर्निर्धनो मानहीन : ।
अल्पायु : स्यात्केद्रणा : पापखेटा ब्रह्मदेषी चापकीतिश्च सर्वे ।।५।।

स्वांशेक्षिते लग्नगते क्रमौशे जीवेन वृष्टे धनराशिपेन ।
व्वनीचभागाविमहीपयोगे जातोपि भूमेरधिपत्यमेति ।। १०।।

एवं चिन्तामणौ ORE केकटेशन धीमता ।
नीधपागादियोगार्थं राजयोगादिज फलम ।।११।।

Even though the location of planets in the Navamsha of their
signs of debilitation in the case of people with Rajayoga, normally
cancels such a yoga, yet if the kendras and trines are occupied by
46 plancts the yoga continues. (9) Similarly. a person with

jayoga having planets located in Navamsha of debilitation, but
having the planet creating Rajayoga in lagna, located in its own
Navamsha is aspected by Jupiter & the lord of the 2nd house. still
gives rulership. (10) Thus the results or Rajayoga for planets in
debilitation Navamsha. (11)

Sun. Mars and Saturn are “dry” planets. Moon and Venus are
watery. Mercury and Jupiter become watery if associated with
watery signs, otherwise they are dry. Aquarius, Cancer. Pisces.
Capricorn. Scorpio, Libra arc watery signs. other signs are without
water. (12-14)

BADHAK

The 9 planets belonging the 9 asterisms at birth are as under &
give results as indicated against each : 1st Sun. heat; 2nd Mercury,
lovely face; 3rd Rahu, losses; 4th Jupiter, possession; Sth Ketu. des-
truction; 6th Moon, fame; 7th Saturn, losses; 8th Venus, dexulta-
tion; 9th Mars, death. In this order Sun. Mercury etc come
every day. वि

The “Badhaka” (frustrative) planets are in the case of people
with movable signs. The planets in the 11th house & the lord of the
11th house, for those having fixed signs as their Ascendants, the
9th house lord & the planets -7 the 9th house & for people having
common signs as their Ascendant, the 7th house lord & the planets `
in the 7th house are Badhakas. The planets, lord of the sign
occupied by the “Kharesh” (22nd decante) & Mandi are nighly
Badhakas (obstructive) karkas (significator) for the 12 houses are
Ist house Sun, 2nd Jupiter, 3rd Mars, 4th Moon & Mercury 5th
Jupiter, 6th Saturn & Mars 7th Venus 8th Saturn, 9th Sun & Jupiter

10th Jupiter, Sun & Mercury 11th Jupiter & 12th Saturn.

TRANSLATOR’S NOTE

Karak for the Ist house is Siin both for health and honour.
Karka i.e. significator for the 2nd house is Jupiter which means in
financial matter. Significator for the 3rd house is Mars which has
to be studied when considering younger brothers. Significator for
the 4th house is Moon in respect of mother, & Mercury in respect
of relatives other than our own family. We can include here Saturn
as the significator of lands & Mars as the significator of built up
property & Venus as the significator for conveyances. Jupiter is the
significawor for the 5th nouse as son. Saturn is significator for the
6th house as disease, white Mars is significator of enemies, litiga-
ton & injunies. Venus is the significator of 7th house as wife.
Saturn is the significator of the 8thshouse as longevity. Sun is
significator of the 9th house as tather & Jupiter as Guru &
governmental favour, Sun is signiticator for the 10th house as
“Ruling” powers. Jupiter & Mercury both can be considered as
significators for acts of charity. Jupiter can be considered as
significator for the 11th house both as the elder brother & as finan-
ces. Saturn can be considered as the significator for the 12th house
as a “Separator”

Sun is significator for father, prowess, health, purity of mind,
liking, spiritual knowledge, Moon is the significator for white
‘coloured chonirie (an item of royal use) fame, pleasure, lustre of
body, beauty of face, mother, mind, & peace. (1-2) Mars is the
significator for bravery, victory, fame, battle, courage. genéralship,
executive power, sword. parshu (axe) adha kunta (spear) kuthar,
guns, bhindpal, efficiency in use of bows & arrows, patience, glow
of face, seriousness, sex, anger, growth of enemies, argumentation,
bad name, freedom of self, the foster mother & earth. (3) Mercury
is the significator for progeny. peace of mind, humility, devotion,
intellect, uncles, relatives, community, prosperty of gotra (family
tree) mathematics, spiritual intellect, knowledge of Vedanta. (4)

Jupiter is the significator for:-

Power of eloquence, Mantras (including advisory capacity)
management of governmental affairs, spiritually established.
elephants, horses, conveyances knowledge of Vedas, karma (good
& bad), son, wealth, means of livelihood. yoga, throne, (5) Venus is
significator for:-

Music, literature, enjoyment of service of others, fine sexual
enjoyments of women and other amorous etc pleasures. Fine
beauty, ruling powers, charming influence, winning over the king.
Knowledge of magic, flowers, excelling others, yagic powers, all
types of wealth & power, enjoyments & wife. (6)

Saturn is significator of greed. attachment, cruel. tormentor of
others. adamant, ill-disposed. poverty, bad condition, disease,
wind. curt speech, buffalow. barley, black grains, longevity, means
of livelihood. (7) Rahu is significator of fame, honour, canopy
etc. (8)
